Smart contract muri RGB ishobora kubonwa nk’imashini ya Leta, isobanurwa na:




- A **Igihugu**, ni ukuvuga urutonde rw’amakuru yerekana uko Contract iteye ubu;
- A **Business Logic** (urutonde rw’amategeko), adondora ingene Leta ishobora guhindurwa n’uwushobora guhindurwa.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/056.webp)


Ni vyiza gutahura ko ayo masezerano atagarukira ku gutanga ibimenyetso vyoroshe. Bishobora gukoresha uburyo bwinshi: kuva ku mutungo wa kera (ibimenyetso, amafaranga, amabondi) gushika ku buhinga bukomeye cane (uburenganzira bwo gukoresha, amajambo y’ubudandaji, n’ibindi). Udakunze izindi blockchains, aho kode ya Contract ishobora gushikwako kandi igashirwa mu ngiro na bose, uburyo bwa RGB buragabanya uburyo bwo gushikira no kumenya Contract ku bari muri iyo nama ("***abaje muri Contract***"). Hariho uruhara rwinshi:




- **Uwutanga** canke umuremyi wa Contract, ni we asigura Genesis ya Contract n'ibihinduka vyayo vy'intango;
- Abafise **uburenganzira** (*Ownership*) canke ubundi bushobozi bwo gushitsa amategeko;
- **Abarorerezi**, bashobora kuba bafise aho babona amakuru amwamye, ariko badashobora gutuma habaho ihinduka.


Ukwo gutandukanya uruhara biratuma habaho ukurwanya ugucengera, mu kumenya ko abantu bemerewe bonyene ari bo bashobora gukorana na Leta y’amasezerano. Iha kandi RGB ubushobozi bwo gupima mu buryo buringaniye: ivyemezo vyinshi bibera hanze ya Blockchain, kandi ni vyo vyonyene bifata amabanga (*amasezerano*) vyanditswe kuri Bitcoin.


### Ikibanza na Business Logic muri RGB


Uvuye ku bijanye n’ibikorwa, **Business Logic** ya Contract ifata uburyo bw’amategeko n’inyandiko, zisobanurwa mu co RGB yita **Schema**. Schema ivuga:




- Imiterere ya Leta (ni imirima iyihe ari iya bose? Ni iyihe mirima ifiswe n’imigambwe iyihe?
- Ivyangombwa vy’uburenganzira (ni igiki kigomba gusuzumwa imbere yo kwemerera Leta guhindura?);
- Ivyemezo (ni nde yoshobora gutanguza *State Transition*? Ni nde yoshobora kwihweza gusa?).


Muri ico gihe nyene, **Contract State** akenshi igabanywamwo ibice bibiri:




- A **Global State**: igice ca bose, gishobora kwihwezwa na bose (bivanye n’imiterere);
- **Ibihugu vy'Igihugu**: ibice vy'abantu ku giti cabo, bigenewe cane cane ba nyen'ibihugu biciye ku ma UTXO yerekanwa mu nzira y'ubwenge ya Contract.


Nk'uko tuzobibona mu bice bikurikira, ivugurura ryose ry'imimerere (*Contract Operation*) ritegerezwa gushirwa ku _nsezerano_ ya Bitcoin (biciye kuri `Opret` canke `Tapret`) kandi ryubahirize inyandiko za *Business Logic* kugira ngo ribonwe ko rifise akamaro.


### Contract Ibikorwa: iremwa n'iterambere rya Leta


Mu gisata ca RGB, ***Contract Operation*** ni ikintu cose gihindura Contract kuva mu **gihugu ca kera** gushika ku **gihugu gishasha**. Ivyo bikorwa bikurikira ubu buhinga bukurikira:




- Turabona uko Contract iri ubu;
- Turashira mu ngiro itegeko canke igikorwa (***State Transition***, ***Genesis*** nimba ari Leta ya mbere cane, canke ***State Extension*** nimba hari *Valency* ya bose yo gusubira gutera);
- Twebwe Anchor ihinduka biciye mu _ukwiyemeza_ gushasha kuri Blockchain, dufunga _ikidodo kimwe co gukoresha rimwe_ tukarema ikindi;
- Abafise uburenganzira baremeza mu karere (*uruhande rw'umukiriya*) ko iyo mpinduka ihuye na *Schema* kandi ko iyo nzira y'ubudandaji ya Bitcoin yanditswe On-Chain.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/057.webp)


Iherezo ry’ivyo ni Contract yahinduwe, ubu ikaba ifise igihugu gitandukanye. Iryo hinduka ntirisaba ko urubuga rwose rwa Bitcoin rwitwararika ido n'ido, kuko urutoke rutoyi gusa (_ukwiyemeza_) rwanditswe muri Blockchain. Urutonde rw’Ibimenyetso vy’Ikoreshwa Rimwe rurabuza Double-spending iyo ari yo yose canke gukoresha kabiri Leta.


### Uruhererekane rw'ibikorwa: kuva kuri Genesis gushika ku gihugu c'iherezo


Kugira ngo ivyo tubishire mu ngiro, RGB Smart contract itangura n’i **Genesis**, igihugu ca mbere nyene. Inyuma y’aho, Ibikorwa bitandukanye vya Contract birakurikirana, bikagira DAG (*Directed Acyclic Graph*) y’ibikorwa:




- Impinduka yose ishingiye ku nkuru y’imbere (canke nyinshi, mu gihe c’impinduka zihuye);
- Urutonde rw’ibihe ruremezwa n’ugushiramwo ihinduka ryose mu gitabu Bitcoin Anchor, gifise ikidodo c’igihe kandi kitahinduka bivuye ku kwumvikana kwa Proof-of-Work;
- Iyo ata bindi bikorwa biriko birakorwa, **Igihugu c'Iherezo** kirashikwako: igihugu gishasha kandi cuzuye ca Contract.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/012.webp)


Iyi topologie ya DAG (aho kuba uruzitiro rworoshe rw’umurongo) yerekana ko bishoboka ko ibice bitandukanye vya Contract bishobora gutera imbere mu buryo bumwe, igihe cose bitavuguruzanya. RGB rero yitwararika kwirinda ukudahuza kwose biciye mu kugenzura *ku ruhande rw’umukiriya* umuntu wese ari muri iyo nama.


### Icegeranyo


Amasezerano y’ubwenge muri RGB azana uburyo bw’ibikoresho vy’ubuhinga bwa none, vyegerejwe ariko bishingiye kuri Bitcoin kugira ngo bimenyeshe igihe no kwemeza urutonde rw’ibikorwa. Ishirwa mu ngiro ry’ayo masezerano rishingiye kuri:




- A **Contract State**, yerekana uko Contract iteye ubu (uburenganzira, uburinganire, ibihinduka, n’ibindi);
- A **Business Logic** (*Schema*), isobanura amahinduka yemerewe n’ingene ategerezwa kwemezwa;
- Ibikorwa vya **Contract**, bihindura iyi leta intambwe ku yindi, bivuye ku masezerano ashingiye ku bikorwa vya Bitcoin.


Mu gice gikurikira, tuzoja mu buryo burambuye ku bijanye n'ukuntu izo ***intara*** n'izo ***intara*** zigaragara ku rugero rwa off-chain, n'ingene zifitaniye isano n'ivyo bimenyetso vy'ubuhinga bwa none (UTXOs) n'ibimenyetso vy'ubuhinga bwa none (Single-use Seals) bishizwe muri Bitcoin. Ivyo bizoba ari akaryo ko kubona ingene ubuhinga bwo mu mutima bwa RGB, bushingiye kuri Client-side Validation, bushobora kuguma buhuye n’amasezerano y’ubwenge mu gihe buzigama ibanga ry’amakuru.


## RGB Ibikorwa vya Contract


<chapterId>78c44e88-50c4-5ec4-befe-456c1a9f080b</chapterId>


:::id ya videwo=1caec34d-f214-425b-a1a4-0a40ae7d3e0e:::


Muri iki gice, turaza kuraba ingene ibikorwa mu masezerano y’ubwenge no mu guhindura Leta bikora, kandi mu gihe c’amasezerano ya RGB. Intumbero izoba kandi iyo gutahura ingene abaje mu nama benshi bafatanya mu gutanga Ownership y’umutungo.


### Impinduka za Leta n'ubuhinga bwazo


Ingingo rusangi iracari iyo muri Client-side Validation, aho amakuru ya Leta afiswe na nyen’ayo makuru, akaremezwa n’uwuyaronka. Ariko rero, ikintu kidasanzwe aha kuri RGB kiri mu kuba Bob, nk’uwuronka, asaba Alice kwinjiza amakuru amwamwe mu makuru ya Contract kugira ngo agire ububasha nyakuri ku mutungo yaronse, biciye ku nsiguro yihishije kuri imwe mu ma UTXO yiwe.


Kugira ngo tubone ingene *State Transition* ikora (ari yo imwe mu nzira z’ishimikiro ***Ibikorwa vya Contract*** muri RGB), reka dufate akarorero k’intambwe ku yindi k’uguhindura umutungo hagati ya Alice na Bob:


**Ivyabaye mu ntango:**


Alice ifise ***Stash RGB*** y’amakuru yemejwe mu karere (*uruhande rw’umukiriya*). Iyi Stash yerekeza kuri imwe mu UTXO ziwe kuri Bitcoin. Ivyo bisigura ko _insobanuro y'ikidodo_ muri aya makuru yerekana UTXO ari iya Alice. Iciyumviro ni ukumushoboza kwimurira uburenganzira bumwe bumwe bujanye n'umutungo (nk'ibimenyetso vya RGB) kuri Bob.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/058.webp)


**Bob nayo irafise ama UTXO:**


Ku rundi ruhande, Bob afise n’imiburiburi UTXO imwe yiwe bwite, ata sano ry’ukuri n’iya Alice. Iyo Bob ata UTXO afise, birashoboka ko yomurungikira akoresheje *Witness Transaction* ubwayo: igisubizo c'iyi nzira kizobamwo Commitment (_commitment_) kandi kizofatanya Ownership ya Bob nshasha na GW-69.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/059.webp)


**Ubwubatsi bw'itongo rishasha (*Leta nshasha*):**


Bob yohereza amakuru ya Alice akodeshejwe mu buryo bwa ***Invoice*** (tuzoja mu ndondoro ku bijanye n'ubwubatsi bwa Invoice mu bice bizokurikira), imusaba kurema igihugu gishasha gihuye n'amategeko ya Contract. Iyi leta izobamwo *Seal Definition* nshasha yerekana imwe mu UTXO za Bob. Muri ubwo buryo, Bob ihabwa Ownership y’itunga risobanuwe muri iyo leta nshasha, nk’akarorero umubare kanaka w’ibimenyetso vya RGB.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/060.webp)


**Gutegura urugero rw'ugucuruza:**


Alice rero irema igikorwa ca Bitcoin ikoresha UTXO yavuzwe muri Seal ya kera (iyo yamuhaye uburenganzira bwo kuba uwuyifise). Mu gisohoka c'iyi nzira, *Commitment* (biciye muri `Opret` canke `Tapret`) yinjizwa muri Anchor igihugu gishasha ca RGB. Amasezerano ya `Opret` canke `Tapret` akomoka ku giti ca *MPC* (nk’uko vyabonetse mu bice vyabanje), gishobora gukoranya amahinduka menshi ava mu masezerano atandukanye.


**Ugutanga *Consignment* kuri Bob:**


Imbere yo gutangaza iyo nzira, Alice yohereza Bob ***Consignment*** irimwo amakuru yose akenewe *yo ku ruhande rw’umukiriya* (*Stash* yiwe) n’amakuru mashasha ya Leta afasha Bob. Muri iki gihe, Bob ikoresha amategeko y’uguhurizako RGB:




- Iremeza amakuru yose ya RGB ari muri *Consignment*, harimwo na Leta nshasha iyiha Ownership y’umutungo;
- Ishingiye ku *Anchors* ziri muri *Consignment*, igenzura urutonde rw'ibikorwa vy'abashingantahe (kuva kuri Genesis gushika ku mpinduka iherutse) kandi ikemeza amasezerano ahuye muri Blockchain.


**Uguheza kw'ihinduka:**


Iyo Bob yuzuye, arashobora gutanga ukwemera kwiwe (nk’akarorero, mu gushira umukono kuri *Consignment*). Alice irashobora rero gutangaza ivyerekanwa vy’ugucuruza vyateguwe. Ivyo bimaze kwemezwa, ivyo bica bifunga Seal yari ifiswe na Alice, bigatuma Ownership igira Bob. Umutekano wo kurwanya Double-spending rero ushingiye ku buryo bumwe nk’ubwo muri Bitcoin: UTXO irakoreshwa, bikaba vyerekana ko Alice itagishobora kuyikoresha.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/061.webp)


Leta nshasha ubu ikoresha Bob ya Bob, igaha Bob Ownership yahora ifiswe na Alice. Igisohoka ca Bitcoin aho amakuru ya RGB ashizweho gica kiba ikimenyamenya kidashobora gusubirwamwo c'ukwimurirwa kwa Ownership.


Akarorero k’i DAG ntoyi (*Directed Acyclic Graph*) igizwe n’ibikorwa bibiri vya Contract (**Genesis** hanyuma ***State Transition***) karashobora kwerekana ingene igihugu ca RGB (*uruhande rw’umukiriya* Layer, mu mutuku) gifatanya na Blockchain4 G4*W-740). mu rurimi rw’umuhondo).


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/062.webp)


Birerekana ko Genesis isobanura Seal (*Seal Definition*), hanyuma *State Transition* igafunga iyo Seal kugira ngo ireme indi nshasha mu yindi UTXO.


Muri ivyo, ng’ibi ivyibutsa bikeyi vy’amajambo:




- ***Assignment*** ihuriza hamwe ibi bikurikira:
    - Indege ***Seal Definition*** (ikaba yerekana indege 755);
- Ibihugu vy'ubutunzi, ni ukuvuga amakuru ahuye na **Ownership** (nk'akarorero, igitigiri c'ibimenyetso vyimuriwe).
- **Global State** ihuriza hamwe imiterere rusangi ya Contract, iboneka kuri bose, kandi igatuma ivy’ubwihindurize bihuye kw’isi yose.


**Impinduka za Leta**, zavuzwe mu kigabane c'imbere, ni zo nzira nyamukuru za Contract Operation. Bivuga intara imwe canke nyinshi za kera (kuva kuri Genesis canke iyindi State Transition) hanyuma zigasubiramwo intara nshasha.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/063.webp)


Iki kigereranyo kirerekana ingene, muri *State Transition Bundle*, ibimenyetso vyinshi bishobora gupfungwa mu gucuruza kw’akarorero kamwe, mu gihe nyene bifungura ibimenyetso bishasha. Nkako, ikintu gishimishije c’umurongo wa RGB ni ubushobozi bwawo bwo gupima: inzira nyinshi zishobora guteranirizwa hamwe zigacika Transition Bundle, iyo nzira yose ikaba ifatanijwe n’ibabi ridasanzwe ry’igiti ca *MPC* (ikimenyetso kidasanzwe c’umugwi). Kubera uburyo bwa *Deterministic Bitcoin Commitment* (DBC), ubutumwa bwose bwinjizwa mu gisohoka ca `Tapret` canke `Opret`, mu gihe bufunga ibimenyetso vya kera kandi bishoboka ko busobanura ibindi bishasha. `Anchor` ikora nk’ihuriro ry’ukuri hagati ya Commitment ibitswe muri Blockchain n’imiterere ya Client-side Validation (*uruhande rw’umukiriya*).


Mu bice bikurikira, turaza kuraba ibice vyose n'ingene bigenda mu kwubaka no kwemeza State Transition. Vyinshi muri ivyo Elements biri mu vyo RGB yemeranije, bishirwa mu ngiro mu **Isoko ry’Ibitabo ry’Ishingiro rya RGB**.


### Transition Bundle


Ku RGB, birashoboka gukoranya Impinduka za Leta zitandukanye ziri muri Contract imwe (ni ukuvuga gusangira **ContractId** imwe, ikomoka kuri Genesis **OpId**). Mu buryo bworoshe, nk’uko biri hagati ya Alice na Bob mu karorero kari hejuru, **Transition Bundle** irimwo inzira imwe gusa. Ariko gushigikira ibikorwa vy’abariha benshi (nk’ama coinjoins, ugufungura imirongo ya Lightning, n’ibindi) bisigura ko abakoresha benshi bashobora gufatanya Impinduka zabo za Leta mu mugwi umwe.


Iyo zimaze kwegeranywa, izo mpinduka zishirwako (n’uburyo bwa MPC + DBC) mu gikorwa kimwe ca Bitcoin:




- State Transition yose irashirwako hashe maze igashirwa mu migwi ikaba Transition Bundle;
- Transition Bundle ubwayo irahashwa maze igashirwa mu ibabi ry’igiti ca MPC rihuye n’iri Contract (BundleId);
- Igiti ca MPC gica gikorana na `Opret` canke `Tapret` muri Witness Transaction, ivyo bikaba bifunga ibimenyetso vyakoreshejwe kandi bikasobanura ibimenyetso bishasha.


Mu buryo bw'ubuhinga, **BundleId** yinjijwe mu rupapuro rwa MPC iboneka ku Hash ikoreshwa ku gukurikirana gukomeye kw'umurima wa *InputMap* w'umugwi:


```txt
BundleId = SHA256( SHA256(bundle_tag) || SHA256(bundle_tag) || InputMap )
```


Mu `umugwi_tag = urn:lnp-bp:RGB:umugwi#2024-02-03` nk'akarorero.


*InputMap* ni urutonde rw'amakuru rutanga urutonde, kuri buri nkuru `i` y'urugero rw'ibikorwa, ivyerekeye *OpId* ya State Transition ihuye. Nk'akarorero:


```txt
InputMap =
N               input_0    OpId(input_0)    input_1    OpId(input_1)   ...    input_N-1  OpId(input_N-1)
|____________________| |_________||______________| |_________||______________|       |__________||_______________|
16-bit Little Endian   32-bit LE   32-byte hash
|_________________________| |_________________________|  ...  |___________________________|

MapElement1                MapElement2                       MapElementN
```




- `N` ni umubare wose w'ibintu vyinjijwe mu gucuruza vyerekeye `OpId`;
- opId(input_j)` ni ikimenyetso c'ibikorwa ca kimwe mu bihinduka vya Leta biri mu mugwi.


Mu gusubiramwo ikintu cose cinjijwe rimwe gusa kandi mu buryo bubereye, turabuza ko Seal imwe ikoreshwa incuro zibiri mu Nzira zibiri z’Igihugu zikora icarimwe.


### Uruvyaro rwa Leta n'Igihugu gikora


Impinduka za Leta rero zirashobora gukoreshwa mu gukura Ownership y'umutungo ku muntu umwe ukayijana ku wundi. Ariko rero, si vyo vyonyene bishobora gukorwa mu masezerano ya RGB. Iryo tegeko risobanura ibikorwa bitatu vya **Contract**:




- 792;
- 793;
- 794.


Muri ivyo, **Genesis** na **State Extension** rimwe na rimwe vyitwa "*Ibikorwa vyo Guhingura Leta*", kuko bihingura Leta nshasha ata n'imwe ihita ifunga. Iyi ni ingingo ihambaye cane: **Genesis** na **State Extension** ntibirimwo gufunga Seal. Ahubwo, basigura Seal nshasha, itegerezwa rero gukoreshwa n’iyindi **State Transition** ikurikira kugira ngo yemezwe vy’ukuri muri kahise ka Blockchain.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/064.webp)


**Igihugu gikora** ca Contract akenshi gisobanurwa nk'umugwi w'ibihugu bishasha biva ku mateka (DAG) y'ibikorwa, gutangura na Genesis bigakurikira ivyuma vyose biri muri Bitcoin Blockchain. Intara zose za kera zisanzwe zitagikoreshwa (i.e. zifatanye n’ama UTXO yakoreshejwe) ntizigifatwa nk’izikora, ariko ziguma ari ngirakamaro mu kugenzura ukuntu amateka ahuye.


### Genesis


Genesis ni intango ya RGB yose Contract. Iremwa n'uwayitanga Contract kandi isobanura ibipimo vy'intango, bihuye na **Schema**. Ku bijanye na RGB token, Genesis ishobora gusobanura, nk’akarorero:




- Igitigiri c’ibimenyetso vyaremwe mu ntango n’ababifise;
- Igitigiri cose c’ibibazo bishoboka;
- Amategeko yose yo gusubira gusohora, n’abaje mu nama bashobora gutora.


Kubera ko ari ryo rya mbere rigurishwa muri Contract, Genesis ntivuga igihugu na kimwe ca kera, eka mbere ntiyifunga Seal iyo ari yo yose. Ariko rero, kugira ngo Genesis iboneke muri kahise kandi yemezwe, itegerezwa **gukoreshwa** (ipfungwa) na State Transition ya mbere (kenshi ni igikorwa co gucapura/kwikoresha ubwaco ku wuyitanga ubwiwe, canke ugutanga ubwa mbere ku bakoresha).


### State Extension


**Ivyiyumviro vya Leta** bitanga ikintu c'umwimerere ku masezerano y'ubwenge. Bituma bishoboka ku Redeem uburenganzira bumwe bumwe bw'ubuhinga bwa none (*Valenties*) buvugwa mu nsobanuro ya Contract, ata gufunga Seal ubwo nyene. Akenshi, ivyo bireba:




- Ibinyamakuru vya token vyatanzwe;
- Uburyo bwo guhindura itunga;
- Gusubira gusohora bifise ivyangombwa (bishobora kubamwo no gusenyura ibindi bintu n’ibindi).


Mu buryo bw’ubuhinga, State Extension yerekeza kuri *Redeem* (ubwoko bumwe bw’inyungu ya RGB) buhuye na *Valency* yasobanuwe mbere (nk’akarorero, muri Genesis canke uwundi State Transition). Irasobanura Seal nshasha, iboneka ku muntu canke ku kibazo kivyungukirako. Kugira ngo iyo Seal ikore, itegerezwa gukoreshwa n’iyindi State Transition ikurikira.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/065.webp)


Nk’akarorero: Genesis irema uburenganzira bwo gutanga (*Valency*). Ivyo bishobora gukorwa n’umukinyi yemerewe, aca yubaka State Extension:




- Rivuga igitabu ca Valency (Redeem);
- Irema *Assignment* nshasha (amakuru mashasha ya *Owned State*) yerekana UTXO;
- State Transition izoza, isohowe na nyen’iyi UTXO nshasha, mu vy’ukuri izokwimurira canke igatanga ivyo bimenyetso bishasha vyasohowe.


### Ibice vy'indege Contract Operation


Ubu rero ndashaka kuraba mu buryo burambuye buri kimwe mu bigize Elements ya **Contract Operation** muri RGB. Contract Operation ni igikorwa gihindura uko Contract imeze, kandi cemezwa ku ruhande rw’umukiriya, mu buryo bugenwa, n’uwuyironka mu buryo bubereye. Cane cane, turabona ingene Contract Operation ifata mu muzirikanyi, ku ruhande rumwe, **ivya kera** vya Contract, ku rundi ruhande, insobanuro ya **ivya kera** .


```txt
+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
|  Contract Operation                                                                                                 |
|                                                                                                                     |
|  +-----+     +-----------------------+      +--------------------------------+      +---------+     +------------+  |
|  | Ffv |     | ContractId | SchemaId |      | TransitionType | ExtensionType |      | Testnet |     | AltLayers1 |  |
|  +-----+     +-----------------------+      +--------------------------------+      +---------+     +------------+  |
|                                                                                                                     |
|  +-----------------------------------------------+  +------------------------------------------------------------+  |
|  | Metadata                                      |  | Global State                                               |  |
|  |                                               |  | +----------------------------------+                       |  |
|  | +-------------------------------------+       |  | | +-------------------+ +--------+ |                       |  |
|  | |          Structured Data            |       |  | | |  GlobalStateType  | |  Data  | |     ...     ...       |  |
|  | +-------------------------------------+       |  | | +-------------------+ +--------+ |                       |  |
|  |                                               |  | +----------------------------------+                       |  |
|  +-----------------------------------------------+  +------------------------------------------------------------+  |         +------+
|                                                                                                                     +---------> OpId |
|  +-----------------------------------------------+  +------------------------------------------------------------+  |         +------+
|  | Inputs                                        |  | Assignments                                                |  |
|  |                                               |  |                                                            |  |
|  | +-------------------------------------------+ |  | +--------------------------------------------------------+ |  |
|  | | Input #1                                  | |  | | Assignment #1                                          | |  |
+------+       |  | | +----------+ +----------------+ +-------+ | |  | | +----------------+ +-------------+ +-----------------+ | |  |       +--------------+
| OpId +--------------> PrevOpId | | AssignmentType | | Index | | |  | | | AssignmentType | | Owned State | | Seal Definition +--------------> Bitcoin UTXO |
+------+       |  | | +----------+ + ---------------+ +-------+ | |  | | +----------------+ +-------------+ +-----------------+ | |  |       +--------------+
|  | +-------------------------------------------+ |  | +--------------------------------------------------------+ |  |
|  |                                               |  |                                                            |  |
|  | +-------------------------------------------+ |  | +--------------------------------------------------------+ |  |
|  | | Input #2                                  | |  | | Assignment #2                                          | |  |
+------+       |  | | +----------+ +----------------+ +-------+ | |  | | +----------------+ +-------------+ +-----------------+ | |  |       +--------------+
| OpId +--------------> PrevOpId | | AssignmentType | | Index | | |  | | | AssignmentType | | Owned State | | Seal Definition +--------------> Bitcoin UTXO |
+------+       |  | | +----------+ +----------------+ +-------+ | |  | | +----------------+ +-------------+ +-----------------+ | |  |       +--------------+
|  | +-------------------------------------------+ |  | +--------------------------------------------------------+ |  |
|  |                                               |  |                                                            |  |
|  |       ...           ...          ...          |  |     ...          ...             ...                       |  |
|  |                                               |  |                                                            |  |
|  +-----------------------------------------------+  +------------------------------------------------------------+  |
|                                                                                                                     |
|  +-----------------------------------------------+  +------------------------------------------------------------+  |
|  | Redeems                                       |  | Valencies                                                  |  |
|  |                                               |  |                                                            |  |
|  | +------------------------------+              |  |                                                            |  |
+------+       |  | | +----------+ +-------------+ |              |  |  +-------------+  +-------------+                          |  |
| OpId +--------------> PrevOpId | | ValencyType | |  ...   ...   |  |  | ValencyType |  | ValencyType |         ...              |  |
+------+       |  | | +----------+ +-------------+ |              |  |  +-------------+  +-------------+                          |  |
|  | +------------------------------+              |  |                                                            |  |
|  |                                               |  |                                                            |  |
|  +-----------------------------------------------+  +------------------------------------------------------------+  |
|                                                                                                                     |

+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
```


Turavye igishushanyo kiri hejuru, turabona ko Contract Operation irimwo Elements yerekeza ku **Leta Nshasha** n’izindi zivuga **Leta ya kera** yahinduwe.


Elements za **Leta Nshasha** ni:




- **Inshingano**, muri zo zisobanurwa:
 - Ivyo **Seal Definition**;
 - Ivyo **Owned State**.
- Ico **Global State**, gishobora guhindurwa canke gutunganirizwa;
- **Ivyiza**, bishobora kuba bisobanuwe muri State Transition canke Genesis.


**Igihugu ca kera** kivugwa biciye kuri:




- **Inputs**, zigaragaza *Ibikorwa* vy'imihindukire ya Leta ya kera (ntibiri muri Genesis);
- **Redeems**, zivuga ku Valencies zasobanuwe mbere (mu Vyagutse vya Leta gusa).


Ikindi, Contract Operation irimwo ibindi bibanza rusangi vyerekeye igikorwa:




- `ffv` (*Verisiyo yihuta*): umubare wose w'amabayiti 2 ugaragaza verisiyo ya Contract;
- `UbwokoBw'Impinduka` canke `UbwokoBw'Ikwaguka`: Umubare w'ibice 16 ugaragaza ubwoko bw'Impinduka canke Ukwaguka, hakurikijwe Business Logic;
- `Id y'amasezerano`: umubare w'amabayiti 32 yerekeye *OpId* ya Contract Genesis. Ishizwe mu Nzira z’Impinduka n’Ivyagutse, ariko ntiziri mu Genesis;
- schemaId: iri muri Genesis gusa, iyi ni Hash y'amabayite 32 iserukira imiterere (*Schema*) ya Contract;
- `Testnet`: Igiharuro kigaragaza nimba uri ku rubuga rwa Testnet canke Mainnet. Genesis gusa;
- `altlayers1`: umuhinduzi ugaragaza ubundi buryo Layer (Sidechain canke ubundi) bukoreshwa ku makuru ya Anchor yongerako Bitcoin. Iriho gusa muri Genesis;
- `metadata`: umwanya ushobora kubika amakuru y'igihe gito, ngirakamaro mu kwemeza Contract igoye, ariko udategerezwa kwandikwa mu mateka y'imimerere ya nyuma.


Ubwa nyuma, ivyo bibanza vyose bihurizwa hamwe n'uburyo bwo gukora hashing, kugira ngo bivemwo ikimenyetso c'urutoke kidasanzwe, `OpId`. Iyi `OpId` ica ishirwa muri Transition Bundle, igatuma ishobora kwemezwa no kwemezwa muri porotokole.


Buri *Contract Operation* rero imenyekana n'igice ca Hash c'amabayite 32 citwa `OpId`. Iyi Hash ibarwa n’i SHA256 Hash y’iyi Elements yose igize igikorwa. Mu yandi majambo, *Contract Operation* yose irafise Commitment yayo y’ibanga, irimwo amakuru yose akenewe kugira ngo umuntu asuzume ukuri n’uko igikorwa gihuye.


RGB Contract rero imenyekana na `ContractId`, ikomoka kuri Genesis `OpId` (kubera ko ata gikorwa c’imbere ya Genesis). Mu majambo nyayo, dufata Genesis `OpId`, tugahindura urutonde rwa byte maze tugakoresha ubuhinga bwa Base58. Ivyo bituma `ContractId` yoroha gukoresha no kumenya.

### Uburyo bwo kuvugurura ivyangombwa n'amabwirizwa


**Contract State** igereranya amakuru yose umurongo wa RGB utegerezwa gukurikirana ku Contract. Igizwe na:




- **Global State** imwe: iki ni igice ca Contract ca bose, co kw'isi yose, kiboneka kuri bose;
- Igihugu kimwe canke vyinshi vy'Umutungo: **Owned State** yose ifatanye n'iyindi Seal yihariye (kandi rero UTXO kuri Bitcoin). Hariho itandukaniro hagati ya:
    - Ibihugu **vya bose**,
    - Ibihugu **vy’abikorera ku giti cabo**.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/066.webp)


*Global State* ishirwa ataco ihinduye muri *Contract Operation* nk'igice kimwe. *Ibihugu vy'Umutungo* bisobanurwa muri *Assignment* yose, iruhande ya *Seal Definition*.


Ikintu nyamukuru kiranga RGB ni uburyo Global State n’Ibihugu vy’Igihugu bihindurwa. Muri rusangi hari ubwoko bubiri bw'inyifato:




- **Mutable**: iyo ikintu c'igihugu kidondowe nk'igihinduka, igikorwa gishasha cose gisubirira igihugu ca kera n'igihugu gishasha. Amakuru ya kera rero abonwa ko ataco amaze;
- **Kwirundanira**: iyo ikintu c'intara gisobanuwe nk'ikirundanira, igikorwa gishasha cose congera amakuru mashasha ku ntara y'imbere, ata kwandikako. Ico bivamwo ni ubwoko bw'amateka yirundanijwe.


Iyo, muri Contract, ikintu ca leta kitasobanuwe nk'igihinduka canke gitera, ico kintu kizoguma ari ubusa ku bikorwa bikurikira (mu yandi majambo, nta verisiyo nshasha z'iki kibanza). Ni Contract Schema (i.e. Business Logic ifise kode) igena nimba Leta (Isi yose canke Iy’Umuntu) ihinduka, ishobora kwirundanira canke idahinduka. Igihe Genesis imaze gusobanurwamwo, ivyo bishobora guhindurwa gusa iyo Contract ubwayo ibirekuriye, nk'akarorero biciye ku State Extension yihariye.


Imbonerahamwe iri musi yerekana ingene ubwoko bumwebumwe bwa Contract Operation bushobora gukoresha (canke kutakoresha) Global State na Owned State:


|                              | Genesis | State Extension | State Transition |
| ---------------------------- |:-----: |:-------------: |:--------------: |
| **Addition of Global State** |    +    |        -        |        +         |
| **Mutation of Global State** |   n/a   |        -        |        +         |
| **Addition of Owned State**  |    +    |        -        |        +         |
| **Mutation of Owned State**  |   n/a   |       No        |        +         |
| **Addition of Valencies**    |    +    |        +        |        +         |


**`+`**: igikorwa gishoboka iyo Schema ya Contract ibirekuriye.


**`-`**: igikorwa kigomba kwemezwa na State Transition ikurikira (State Extension yonyene ntifunga Single-Use Seal).


Ikindi, urugero rw’igihe n’uburenganzira bwo guhindura ubwoko bumwebumwe bw’amakuru birashobora gutandukanywa mu mbonerahamwe ikurikira:


|                        | Metadata                                | Global State                                     | Owned State                                                                                              |
| ---------------------- | --------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------ | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Scope**              | Defined for a single Contract Operation | Defined globally for the contract                | Defined for each seal (*Assignment*)                                                                     |
| **Who can update it?** | Non-updatable (ephemeral data)          | Operation issued by actors (issuer, etc.)        | Depends on the legitimate holder who owns the seal (the one who can spend it in a following transaction) |
| **Temporal Scope**     | Only for the current operation          | State is established at the end of the operation | State is defined before the operation (by the *Seal Definition* of the previous operation)               |


### Global State


Global State akenshi idondorwa ngo "nta n'umwe ayifise, bose barabizi". Irimwo amakuru rusangi yerekeye Contract, ikaba iboneka ku mugaragaro. Nk’akarorero, mu Contract itanga token, birashoboka ko irimwo:




- Igiharuro (inyuguti ngufi y’ikigereranyo ya token): `igiharuro`;
- Izina ryose rya token: `izina`;
- Ugushikama (umubare w'ibibanza vy'icumi): `ugushikama`;
- Ivyo gutanga vya mbere (na/canke umupaka w’agaciro kanini wa token): `Itangazwa`;
- Itariki y'isohoka: `yaremwe`;
- Amakuru y'amategeko canke ayandi makuru ya bose: `amakuru`.


Iyi Global State ishobora gushirwa ku bikoresho vya bose (imbuga ngurukanabumenyi, IPFS, Nostr, Torrent, n’ibindi) igashikirizwa abantu bose. Kandi, inguvu z’ubutunzi (ugukenera gufata no gutanga ivyo bimenyetso, n’ibindi) ni vyo bituma abakoresha Contract bo ubwabo babungabunga no gukwiragiza ayo makuru.


### Ibikorwa


*Assignment* ni umubumbe w'ishimikiro wo gusobanura:




- Igikoresho ca Seal (*Igikoresho ca Seal Definition*), kigaragaza igikoresho ca UTXO kidasanzwe;
- *Owned State*, ni ukuvuga umutungo canke amakuru ajanye n'iyi Seal.


*Assignment* ishobora kubonwa nk’ikigereranyo c’igisohoka c’ugucuruza ca Bitcoin, ariko ikaba ifise ubushobozi bwo guhinduranya. Aha niho hari uburyo bwo kwimurira umutungo: *Assignment* ifatanya ubwoko bumwe bw'umutungo canke uburenganzira (`Ubwoko bw'Igikorwa`) na Seal. Uwufise urufunguzo rw’ibanga rwa UTXO rufatanye n’iyi Seal (canke uwushobora gukoresha iyi UTXO) afatwa ko ari nyen’iyi *Owned State*.


Kimwe mu bintu bikomeye bikomeye vya RGB ni ubushobozi bwo *guhishura* canke guhisha (*guhisha*) imirima ya *Seal Definition* na *Owned State* uko ushaka. Ivyo bitanga uruvange rukomeye rw’ibanga n’uguhitamwo. Nk’akarorero, urashobora kwemeza ko ihinduka rifise akamaro ata makuru yose utangaje, mu gutanga verisiyo yahishuriwe ku muntu ategerezwa kuyishingira intahe, mu gihe abandi bantu babona gusa verisiyo yihishije (Hash). Mu bikorwa, `OpId` y'ihinduka yama ibarwa ivuye ku makuru *hishijwe*.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/067.webp)


#### Seal Definition


*Seal Definition*, mu buryo bwayo bwahishuriwe, ifise ivyicaro bine vy'ishimikiro: `txptr`, `vout`, `uguhuma` na `uburyo`:




- **txptr**: ibi ni ivyerekeye UTXO kuri Bitcoin:
    - Ku bijanye n’indege **Genesis Seal**, yerekana ata guca ku ruhande UTXO iriho (iyo ifatanye n’iyo Genesis);
    - Mu gihe c'**Igishushanyo Seal**, dushobora kugira:
        - `txid` yoroshe, iyo yerekana UTXO yihariye,
        - Canke `WitnessTx`, yerekana ikintu umuntu yishingirako: Seal yerekana igikorwa ubwaco. Ivyo birakenewe cane cane iyo ata UTXO yo hanze iriho, nk'akarorero mu gufungura umurongo wa Lightning, canke iyo uwuronka ata UTXO afise.
- **vout**: umubare w'isohoka ry'ibikorwa vyerekanywe na `txptr`. Itangazwa gusa ku gishushanyo gisanzwe Seal (si ku `IcabonaTx`);
- **blinding**: umubare w'ibintu 8 vy'ibanga, kugira ngo hakomezwe ibanga no kubuza gukoresha inguvu z'agahomerabunwa ku bijanye n'akaranga ka UTXO;
- **uburyo**: yerekana uburyo bwo gushingira intahe bukoreshwa (`Tapret` canke `Opret`).


Igishushanyo *cahishijwe* ca Seal Definition ni SHA256 Hash (gifise ikimenyetso) c'uguhuza ivyo bibanza 4, gifise ikimenyetso kidasanzwe kuri RGB.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/068.webp)


#### Leta zifise


Igice ca kabiri ca *Assignment* ni Owned State. Udakunze Global State, ishobora kubaho mu buryo bwa bose canke bw’abantu ku giti cabo:




- **Owned State ya bose**: umuntu wese arazi amakuru ajanye na Seal. Nk'akarorero, ishusho y'abantu bose;
- **Private Owned State**: amakuru aranyegezwa, amenyekana gusa na nyen'ayo makuru (kandi bishoboka ko ari uwuyashingira intahe iyo bikenewe). Nk'akarorero, igitigiri c'ibimenyetso bifise.


RGB isobanura ubwoko bune bw'intara bushoboka (*UbwokoBw'intara*) bwa Owned State:




- **Itangazo**: nta makuru y'imibare arimwo, uburenganzira bwo gutangaza gusa (nk'uburenganzira bwo gutora). Ivyo bihishijwe n'ivyo bihishuwe birasa;
- **Fungible**: igereranya umubare ushobora guhinduka (nk'ibimenyetso). Mu buryo bwahishuriwe, dufise `umubare` n'`uguhuma`. Mu buryo bwihishije, dufise *Pedersen commitment* imwe ihisha umubare n'uguhuma amaso;
- **Itunganijwe**: ibika amakuru atunganijwe (gushika kuri 64 kB). Mu buryo bwahishuriwe, ni data blob. Mu buryo bwihishije, ni Hash y'iki gice:


```txt
SHA-256(SHA-256(tag_data) || SHA-256(tag_data) || blob)
```


Na, nk'akarorero:


```txt
tag_data = urn:lnp-bp:rgb:state-data#2024-02-12
```




- **Ivyashizweko**: bihuza dosiye (amajwi, ishusho, bibiri, n'ibindi) na Owned State, bikabika dosiye Hash `file_hash`, ubwoko bwa MIME `ubwoko bw'amakuru` n'umunyu w'ibanga `umunyu`. Dosiye ubwayo iracumbikirwa ahandi. Mu buryo bwihishije, ni Hash ifise ikimenyetso c'ibintu bitatu bibanza:


```txt
SHA-256(SHA-256(tag_attachment) || SHA-256(tag_attachment) || file_hash || media_type || salt)
```


Na, nk'akarorero:


```txt
tag_attachment = urn:rgb:state-attach#2024-02-12
```


Mu ncamake, ng’ubu ubwoko 4 bushoboka bwa Leta mu buryo bwa bose no mu buryo bwihishije:


```txt
State                      Concealed form                              Revealed form

+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
|                                                                                |
Declarative        |                              < void >                                          |
|                                                                                |
+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

+--------------------------+             +---------------------------------------+
| +----------------------+ |             |         +--------+ +----------+       |
Fungible           | | Pedersen Commitement | | <========== |         | Amount | | Blinding |       |
| +----------------------+ |             |         +--------+ +----------+       |
+--------------------------+             +---------------------------------------+

+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

+--------------------------+             +---------------------------------------+
| +----------------------+ |             |         +--------------------+        |
Structured         | |     Tagged Hash      | | <========== |         |     Data Blob      |        |
| +----------------------+ |             |         +--------------------+        |
+--------------------------+             +---------------------------------------+

+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

+--------------------------+             +---------------------------------------+
| +----------------------+ |             | +-----------+ +------------+ +------+ |
Attachments        | |     Tagged Hash      | | <========== | | File Hash | | Media Type | | Salt | |
| +----------------------+ |             | +-----------+ +------------+ +------+ |

+--------------------------+             +---------------------------------------+

```



| **Element**     | **Declarative** | **Fungible**                      | **Structured**       | **Attachments**        |
| --------------- | --------------- | --------------------------------- | -------------------- | ---------------------- |
| **Data**        | None            | Signed or unsigned 64-bit integer | Any strict data type | Any file               |
| **Info Type**   | None            | Signed or unsigned                | Strict types         | MIME Type              |
| **Privacy**     | Not required    | Pedersen commitment               | Hash with blinding   | Hashed file identifier |
| **Size Limits** | N/A             | 256 bytes                         | Up to 64 KB          | Up to ~500 GB          |


### Injiza


Ivyo Inputs za *Contract Operation* vyerekeye *Ibikorwa* biriko birakoreshwa muri iki gikorwa gishasha. Injiza yerekana:




- `prevOpId`: ikimenyetso (`OpId`) c'igikorwa c'imbere aho *Assignment* yari;
- `UbwokoBw'Igikorwa`: ubwoko bwa *Assignment* (nk'akarorero, `Nyitungo` ku token);
- `Index`: urutonde rwa *Assignment* ruri ku rutonde rujanye n'i `OpId` y'imbere, rugenwa inyuma y'ugutoranya kw'inkoranyabumenyi kw'ibimenyetso vyihishijwe.


Ivyinjira ntivyigera biboneka muri Genesis, kuko ata Mirimo y’imbere iriho. Eka mbere ntiziboneka mu Vyagutse vya Leta (kuko Ivyagutse vya Leta bitafunga ibimenyetso; ahubwo, bisubira gusobanura ibimenyetso bishasha bishingiye ku Valencies).


Iyo dufise Owned States z’ubwoko bwa `Fungible`, ubuhinga bwo kwemeza (biciye mu nyandiko ya AluVM itangwa muri Schema) burasuzuma ukuntu imibare ihuye: umubare w’ibimenyetso vyinjira (*Inputs*) utegerezwa kuba ungana n’umubare w’ibimenyetso bisohoka (mu *As* nshasha).


### Amakuru


**Metadata** field ishobora gushika kuri 64 KiB kandi ikoreshwa mu gushiramwo amakuru y'igihe gito ngirakamaro mu kwemeza, ariko ntashizwe mu gihe c'ubudasiba ca Contract. Nk'akarorero, ibihinduka vy'imibare yo hagati y'inyandiko zikomeye birashobora kubikwa hano. Ico kibanza ntikigenewe kubikwa mu mateka y'isi yose, ni co gituma kiri hanze y'ububasha bw'Ibihugu vy'Igihugu canke Global State.


### Ivyiza


**Ivyiyumviro** ni uburyo bw'umwimerere bw'amasezerano ya RGB. Bishobora gusangwa muri Genesis, Impinduka za Leta canke Impinduka za Leta. Bigereranya uburenganzira bw’imibare bushobora gukoreshwa na State Extension (biciye muri *Redeems*), hanyuma bikarangizwa n’Impinduka ikurikira. Buri Valency imenyekana n'`UbwokoBw'Uburemere` (ibice 16). Insobanuro yayo (uburenganzira bwo gusubira gusohora, guhindura token, uburenganzira bwo guturira, n'ibindi) zisobanurwa muri Schema.


Mu majambo nyayo, twoshobora kwiyumvira Genesis isobanura "uburenganzira bwo gusubira gusohora" Valency. State Extension izoyirya (*Redeem*) iyo hari ibintu bimwe bimwe bishitse, kugira ngo haboneke umubare mushasha w’ibimenyetso. Hanyuma, State Transition iva ku wufise Seal yaremwe gutyo irashobora kwimurira ivyo bimenyetso bishasha.


### Gucungura


Ivyo gucungura ni Valency bingana n’Ivyinjira mu bikorwa. Biboneka gusa mu Vyagutse vya Leta, kuko ni ho Valency yari yarasobanuwe mbere ikoreshwa. Redeem igizwe n’ibice bibiri:




- `PrevOpId`: `OpId` y'igikorwa aho Valency yari yaravuzwe;
- `UbwokoBw'Ubushobozi`: ubwoko bwa Valency wipfuza gukoresha (buri `UbwokoBw'Ubushobozi` bushobora gukoreshwa rimwe gusa na State Extension).


Akarorero: Redeem ishobora guhura n'ugushirwa mu ngiro kwa CoinSwap, bivanye n'ivyo vyari vyashizwe muri Valency.


### Ibiranga ikibanza ca RGB


Ubu tugiye kuraba ibiranga Leta vyinshi vy'ishimikiro muri RGB. Cane cane, turaza kuraba:




- **Uburyo bw’ubwoko bukomeye**, butegeka gutunganya amakuru mu buryo bubereye kandi bufise ubwoko;
- Akamaro ko gutandukanya **kwemeza** na **Ownership**;
- Uburyo bwa **ugutera imbere kw'uguhurizako** muri RGB, burimwo ivyiyumviro vy'*ugutera imbere vyihuta* n'*ugusubira inyuma*.


Nk’uko bisanzwe, uzirikane ko ikintu cose gifitaniye isano n’ivy’uburenganzira bwa Contract cemezwa ku ruhande rw’umukiriya hakurikijwe amategeko y’uguhurizako ashizweho mu masezerano, kandi ko ishingiro ryayo ry’iherezo ry’ubuhinga bwa none rishingiye ku bikorwa vya Bitcoin.


#### Ubwoko bukomeye


RGB ikoresha *Ubwoko bukomeye* n'uburyo bwo gukurikirana (*Ugushiramwo amakuru*). Iryo shirahamwe ryagenewe gutuma amakuru ya Contract ashobora gusubirwamwo neza kandi akagira ukuri mu gusobanura, gukoresha no kwemeza.


Mu bidukikije vyinshi vy’iporogarama (JSON, YAML...), imiterere y’amakuru irashobora guhinduka, mbere n’ugushobora kwemera cane. Ku rundi ruhande, muri RGB, Imiterere n’Ubwoko bw’umurima wose birasobanurwamwo ibintu bigaragara. Nk'akarorero:




- Ihinduka ryose rifise ubwoko bwihariye (nk'akarorero, umubare w'ibice 8 udafise ikimenyetso `u8`, canke umubare w'ibice 16 ufise ikimenyetso, n'ibindi);
- Ubwoko burashobora gukorwa (ubwoko bushizwemwo). Ibi bisigura ko ushobora gusobanura ubwoko bushingiye ku bundi bwoko (nk'ubwoko bw'umugwi burimwo umwanya `u8`, umwanya `bool`, n'ibindi);
- Amakoraniro arashobora kandi gusobanurwamwo: urutonde (*urutonde*), imigwi (*imigwi*) canke inkoranyamagambo (*ikarita*), n'urutonde rw'iterambere ry'ibintu;
- Buri murima urafise urubibi (*urubibi rwo hasi* / *urubibi rwo hejuru*). Turashiraho kandi imipaka ku mubare w’ama Elements mu makoraniro (ugukingira);
- Amakuru ni byte-aligned kandi urutonde rurasobanuwe neza kandi rudasobanutse.


Urakoze kuri iyi porotokole y'ugushiramwo amakuru:




- Urutonde rw’ibibanza rwama ari rumwe, ata kuraba ururimi rwo gushirwa mu ngiro canke rwo gukora porogarama rukoreshwa;
- Ivyo biharuro biharuwe ku rutonde rumwe rero birashobora gusubirwamwo kandi birasa (*imihigo* y’ugushingira intahe);
- Imipaka ibuza iterambere ritagenzuwe mu bunini bw’amakuru (nk’akarorero, imirima myinshi cane);
- Ubwo buryo bwo gushiramwo amakuru buratuma habaho ugusuzuma kw’ibanga, kuko umwe wese mu bari muri iyo nyigisho azi neza ingene yoshiramwo amakuru mu rutonde no gukora Hash.


Mu bikorwa, imiterere (*Schema*) n’itegeko rivamwo (*Interface* n’ubwenge bujanye n’ivyo) birakoranirizwa hamwe. Ururimi rudondora rukoreshwa mu gusobanura Contract (ubwoko, ivyicaro, amategeko) na generate uburyo bukomeye bw’ibice bibiri. Iyo bishizwe hamwe, igisubizo ni:




- A *Igishushanyo c'Ukwibuka* ku murima wose;
- Ivyerekana insobanuro (vyerekana nimba guhindura izina ry’igihinduka bifise ingaruka ku nsiguro, naho nyene imiterere y’ukwibuka yoguma ari imwe).


Uburyo bw’ubwoko bukomeye kandi burashoboza gukurikirana neza amahinduka: uguhindura kwose kw’imiterere (mbere n’uguhindura izina ry’umurima) kuramenyekana kandi gushobora gutuma haba uguhinduka kw’ikirenge cose.


Ubwa nyuma, ihuriro ryose ritanga ikimenyetso c’urutoke, ikimenyetso c’ibanga gishingira intahe verisiyo nyayo y’iyo kode (amakuru, amategeko, kwemeza). Akarorero, ikimenyetso c'ifomu:


```txt
BEiLYE-am9WhTW1-oK8cpvw4-FEMtzMrf-mKocuGZn-qWK6YF#ginger-parking-nirvana
```


Ivyo bituma bishoboka gucunga ivyagezwe vy’uguhurizako canke ivy’ugushirwa mu ngiro, mu gihe bishoboka ko umuntu ashobora gukurikirana mu buryo burambuye amaverisiyo akoreshwa mu rubuga.


Kugira ngo ubuzima bwa RGB Contract ntibube bugoye cane ku ruhande rw’umukiriya, itegeko ry’uguhurizako rishiraho ubunini burenze `2^16` bytes (64 Kio) ku makuru yose ari mu biharuro vy’ukwemeza. Ivyo bireba umuhinduzi canke imiterere yose: ntibirenze 65536 bytes, canke ibihwanye n’ivyo mu mibare (32768 16-bit integers, n’ibindi). Ivyo birareba kandi amakoraniro (urutonde, amatsinda, amakarata), adashobora kurenga `2^16` Elements.


Iyi nzira iremeza:




- Igenzura ubunini burengeye ubw’amakuru azokoreshwa mu gihe ca State Transition;
- Uguhuza n'imashini y'ivy'impwemu (*AluVM*) ikoreshwa mu gukoresha inyandiko zo kwemeza.


#### Ivyemezo != Ownership akarorero


Kimwe mu bintu bikomeye RGB yakoze ni ugutandukanya cane ivyiyumviro bibiri:




- **Kwemeza**: kugenzura ko State Transition yubaha amategeko ya Contract (Business Logic, amateka, n'ibindi);
- Ico **Ownership** (Ownership, canke ubugenzuzi): ukuri ko umuntu afise Bitcoin UTXO ishobora gutuma Single-Use Seal ikoreshwa (canke igafungwa), gutyo State Transition ikabaho.


**Ukwemeza** bibera ku rugero rw'ikirundo ca porogaramu RGB (amasomero, *amasezerano*, n'ibindi). Uruhara rwayo ni ugutuma amategeko yo mu mutima yo muri Contract (amahera, uruhusha n’ibindi) yubahirizwa. Abarorerezi canke abandi bari muri iyo nama na bo nyene barashobora kwemeza amateka y’amakuru.


**Ownership**, ku rundi ruhande, yizigiye gusa umutekano wa Bitcoin. Kugira urufunguzo rw’ibanga rwa UTXO bisigura kugenzura ubushobozi bwo gutanguza ihinduka rishasha (gufunga Single-Use Seal). Rero, naho umuntu yoshobora kubona canke kwemeza amakuru, ntashobora guhindura Leta iyo atagira UTXO ireba.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/069.webp)


Ubu buryo buragabanya ubugoyagoye bwa kera buboneka mu bice vy’ubuhinga bikomeye cane (aho kode yose ya Smart contract ari iya bose kandi ishobora guhindurwa n’umuntu wese, ivyo bikaba vyatumye rimwe na rimwe habaho ubusuma). Ku RGB, uwutera ntashobora gusa gukorana na Leta ya On-Chain, kuko uburenganzira bwo gukora kuri Leta (*Ownership*) burindwa na Bitcoin Layer.


Ikindi, uku gutandukanya bituma RGB ishobora kwifatanya na Lightning Network. Imirongo y’umuravyo ishobora gukoreshwa mu gukorana no kwimurira ivy’ubutunzi vya RGB ata gukorana n’*imihigo* ya On-Chain igihe cose. Tuzokwihweza neza uku gushiramwo RGB ku Muravyo mu bice bizokurikira vy’amashure.


#### Iterambere ry'ubumwe muri RGB


Uretse guhindura kode y’insobanuro, RGB irimwo uburyo bwo guhindura canke guhindura amategeko y’uguhurizako ya Contract uko igihe kigenda kirarenga. Hari uburyo bubiri nyamukuru bw'ubwihindurize:




- **Kwihuta-imbere**
- **Gusunika-inyuma**


Ivyihuta gutera imbere bishika iyo itegeko ryari ritagira akamaro mbere rigira akamaro. Nk'akarorero, iyo Contract ihinduka kugira ngo yemere ubwoko bushasha bwa `AssignmentType` canke umwanya mushasha:




- Ivyo ntibishobora kugereranywa n’ivyuma bikomeye vya kera vya Blockchain, kuko RGB ikora muri Client-side Validation kandi ntigira ico ikoze ku bijanye n’uguhuza muri rusangi kwa Blockchain;
- Mu majambo y’ibikorwa, ubwo bwoko bw’ihinduka bugaragazwa n’umwanya `Ffv` (*verisiyo y’imbere yihuta*) muri Contract Operation;
- Abafise ubu ntibagirirwa nabi: ikibanza cabo kiraguma gifise akamaro;
- Ku rundi ruhande, abashasha bazoronka inyungu (canke abakoresha bashasha), barakeneye guhindura porogarama zabo (Wallet yabo) kugira ngo bamenye ayo mategeko mashasha.


Gusubira inyuma bisigura ko itegeko ryari rifise akamaro mbere rihinduka ubusa. Ni rero "ugukomantaza" amategeko, ariko si mu kuvuga ataco twishimikije:




- Abafise ivy’ubutunzi bariho bashobora gushikirwa n’ingorane (boshobora kwisanga bafise ivy’ubutunzi vyahinduwe bitagira akamaro canke bitagira akamaro muri verisiyo nshasha);
- Turashobora kubona ko mu vy’ukuri turiko turarema umurongo mushasha: uwuzokwemera itegeko rishasha aca ava ku rya kera;
- Uwutanga ashobora gufata ingingo yo gusubira gutanga itunga muri iyo porotokole nshasha, agahatira abakoresha kuguma bafise amasakoshi abiri atandukanye (imwe y’iporotokole ya kera, iyindi y’iyindi nshasha), nimba bashaka gucunga izo verisiyo zompi.


Muri iki gice kivuga ku bikorwa vya RGB Contract, twasuzumye ingingo ngenderwako z’ishimikiro zishingiye kuri iyi porotokole. Nk’uko muzoba mwabibonye, ​​ukuntu umurongo wa RGB ugoranye cane bisaba ko hakoreshwa amajambo menshi y’ubuhinga. Rero, mu kigabane gikurikira, nzobaha urutonde rw'amajambo ruzoca irya n'ino ivyiyumviro vyose bivugwa muri iki gice ca mbere c'inyigisho, n'insobanuro z'amajambo yose y'ubuhinga yerekeye RGB. Hanyuma, mu gice gikurikira, tuzokwihweza mu buryo ngirakamaro insobanuro n’ugushirwa mu ngiro kw’amasezerano ya RGB.


## RGB Insobanuro y'amajambo


<chapterId>545e16a4-3cca-44a3-9fd5-dbc5868abf97</chapterId>


Niba ukeneye kugaruka muri uru rutonde rugufi rw’amajambo y’ubuhinga ahambaye akoreshwa mw’isi ya RGB (yashizwe ku rutonde rw’inyuguti), uzosanga ari ngirakamaro. Iki gice si ngombwa nimba umaze gutahura ivyo twavuze vyose mu gice ca mbere.


#### AluVM


Inyuguti ngufi AluVM ihagarariye "_Imashini y'ubuhinga bwa none_", imashini y'ubuhinga bwa none ishingiye ku nzira y'ubuhinga bwa none yagenewe kwemeza Smart contract no gukoresha ubuhinga bwa none. Ikoreshwa (ariko ntiyihariye gusa) mu kwemeza amasezerano ya RGB. Ivyanditswe canke ibikorwa biri muri RGB Contract birashobora rero gukorwa mu bidukikije vya AluVM.


Ushaka kumenya vyinshi: [Urubuga rwemewe rwa AluVM]


#### Anchor


Anchor igereranya urutonde rw'amakuru y'uruhande rw'umukiriya akoreshwa mu kwemeza ko hariho _ukwiyemeza_ kwihariye mu gucuruza. Mu masezerano ya RGB, Anchor igizwe n’ibi bikurikira:




- Igiharuro c’ibikorwa vy’ubudandaji (txid) c’i **Witness Transaction**;
- Ivyo **Multi Protocol Commitment (MPC)**;
- Ivyo **Igitabu-1058 (DBC)**;
- **Ikimenyamenya c'Ibikorwa vy'Iyongera (ETP)** iyo uburyo bwa **Tapret** Commitment bukoreshejwe (raba igice kigenewe iki kigereranyo).


Anchor rero ikoreshwa mu gushinga isano rishobora kugenzurwa hagati y’ugucuruza kwihariye kwa Bitcoin n’amakuru y’ibanga yemejwe n’amasezerano ya RGB. Biremeza ko ayo makuru ari muri Blockchain vy’ukuri, ata vyo arimwo vy’ukuri bimenyeshwa abantu bose.


#### Assignment


Mu nzira ya RGB, Assignment ni nk'igisubizo c'ibikorwa bihindura, bihindura canke bikora ibintu bimwe bimwe mu gihe ca Contract. Igikoresho ca Assignment gifise ama Elements abiri:




- A **Seal Definition** (ivyerekeye UTXO yihariye);
- An **Owned State** (amakuru adondora igihugu gifitaniye isano n’uwo nyen’itongo rishasha).


Assignment rero yerekana ko igice ca Leta (nk’akarorero, umutungo) ubu gihabwa uwufise, kimenyekana biciye ku Single-Use Seal ifatanye na UTXO.


#### Business Logic


Business Logic ihuriza hamwe amategeko yose n’imikorere yo mu mutima ya Contract, idondorwa na **Schema** yayo (ni ukuvuga imiterere ya Contract ubwayo). Irategeka ingene igihugu ca Contract gishobora guhinduka, kandi mu bihe ibihe.


#### Client-side Validation


Client-side Validation yerekeza ku buryo buri ruhande (umukiriya) asuzuma urutonde rw’amakuru ahindurwa mu bwiherero, hakurikijwe amategeko y’amasezerano. Ku bijanye na RGB, ayo makuru yahinduwe ashirwa hamwe mu vyo bita **ivyoherezwa**. Udakunze umurongo wa Bitcoin, usaba ko amafaranga yose akoreshwa atangazwa On-Chain, RGB yemera gusa _imigambi_ (ishingiye kuri Bitcoin) kubikwa mu ruhame, mu gihe amakuru y'ingenzi ya Contract asigaye hagati ya On-Chain, ibimenyamenya gusa) ivyerekeye.


#### Commitment


Commitment (mu buryo bw'ibanga) ni ikintu c'imibare, kigaragazwa na `C`, kiva ku gikorwa ku makuru atunganijwe `m` (ubutumwa) n'agaciro k'imburakimazi `r`. Twandika:


$$
C = \text{commit}(m, r)
$$


Ubu buryo bugizwe n'ibikorwa bibiri nyamukuru:




- **Commit**: igikorwa c'ibanga gikoreshwa ku butumwa `m` n'umubare w'imburakimazi `r` kugira ngo uvemwo `C`;
- **Verify**: dukoresha `C`, ubutumwa `m` n'agaciro ka `r` kugira ngo tugenzure ko iyi Commitment ari ukuri. Igikorwa kigarura `Ukuri` canke `Ikinyoma`.


Commitment itegerezwa kwubahiriza ibintu bibiri:




- **Binding**: bitegerezwa kuba bidashoboka kuronka ubutumwa bubiri butandukanye butanga `C` imwe:


$$
m': \, | \,: m' \neq m \quad \text{and} \quad r': \, | \,: r' \neq r \quad
$$


Nka nka:


$$
\text{verify}(m, r, C) = \text{verify}(m', r', C) \rightarrow \text{True}
$$




- **Kwihisha**: ubumenyi bwa `C` ntibutegerezwa guhishura ibirimwo muri `m`.


Mu masezerano ya RGB, Commitment ishirwa mu gikorwa ca Bitcoin kugira ngo yerekane ko hari amakuru kanaka ariho mu gihe kinaka, ata makuru ubwayo ahishuriwe.


#### Consignment


A **Consignment** ihuriza hamwe amakuru yashikirijwe hagati y'ababuranyi, hakurikijwe Client-side Validation muri RGB. Hariho ivyiciro bibiri nyamukuru vya Consignment:




- **Contract Consignment**: itangwa n'uwutanga (uwatanga Contract), irimwo amakuru y'intango nka Schema, Genesis, Interface na Interface Implementation.
- **Kwimurira Consignment**: bitangwa n'uwuriha (*uwuriha*). Irimwo amateka yose y'impinduka za Leta zishikana ku Terminal Consignment (ni ukuvuga Leta ya nyuma yaronse n'uwuyitanga).


Ivyo bintu birungitswe ntivyandikwa ku mugaragaro ku rupapuro rwa Blockchain; birahanahana ata guca ku ruhande hagati y’ababijejwe biciye ku nzira y’itumanaho bahisemwo.


#### Contract


Contract ni urutonde rw’uburenganzira bushirwa mu ngiro mu buryo bwa digitale hagati y’abakozi benshi biciye ku masezerano ya RGB. Ifise igihugu gikora na Business Logic, isobanurwa na Schema, igaragaza ibikorwa vyemewe (uguhindura, kwongera, n’ibindi). Ivyo Contract imeze, hamwe n'amategeko agenga ukuri kwayo, bivugwa muri Schema. Igihe cose, Contract iratera imbere gusa bivanye n’ivyo vyemewe n’iyi Schema be n’inyandiko zo kwemeza (run, nk’akarorero, muri AluVM).


#### Contract Operation


Contract Operation ni uguhindura ivy’imimerere ya Contract gukorwa hakurikijwe amategeko ya Schema. Ibikorwa bikurikira biri muri RGB:




- 1117;
- 1118;
- 1119.


Igikorwa kimwekimwe cose gihindura igihugu mu kwongerako canke gusubirira amakuru amwamwe (Global State, Owned State...).


#### Contract Participant


Contract Participant ni umukinyi agira uruhara mu bikorwa bijanye na Contract. Muri RGB, hariho itandukaniro hagati ya:




- Uwutanga Contract, ari we arema Genesis (inkomoko ya Contract);
- Abagize Contract, ni ukuvuga abafise uburenganzira ku gihugu ca Contract;
- Amashirahamwe ya Leta, ashobora kwubaka Ivyumba vya Leta iyo Contract itanga Ivyumba vy’Igihugu bishobora gushikirwa na bose.


#### Contract Rights


Contract Rights yerekeza ku burenganzira butandukanye bushobora gukoreshwa n’abafise uruhara muri RGB Contract. Bica mu mice myinshi:




- uburenganzira bwa **Ownership**, bujanye n'uburenganzira bwa Ownership bwa UTXO kanaka (biciye mu _Nsobanuro y'Ikidodo_);
- Uburenganzira bw'ubutegetsi, ni ukuvuga ubushobozi bwo kwubaka inzira imwe canke nyinshi (Inzira za Leta) hakurikijwe Schema;
- **Uburenganzira bwa bose**, iyo Schema yemerera gukoresha ibintu bimwe bimwe vya bose, nk'akarorero kurema State Extension biciye mu gucungura Valency.


#### Contract State


Contract State ihuye n’ingene Contract iri ubu mu gihe kanaka. Ishobora kuba igizwe n'amakuru ya bose n'ay'abikorera ku giti cabo, yerekana uko Contract imeze. RGB itandukanya:




- **Global State**, irimwo ivy’abantu bose vya Contract (vyashizweho muri Genesis canke vyongeweko biciye mu guhindura vyemewe);
- Ibihugu bifise uburenganzira, ari vyo vy'abafise uburenganzira bwihariye, bimenyekana n'ama UTXO yabo.


#### Deterministic Bitcoin Commitment - DBC


Deterministic Bitcoin Commitment (DBC) ni urutonde rw'amategeko akoreshwa mu kwandika mu buryo bugaragara kandi budasanzwe _ukwiyemeza_ mu gucuruza Bitcoin. Mu masezerano ya RGB, hari uburyo bubiri nyamukuru bwa DBC:




- **Gufungura**
- **Tapret**


Ubu buryo burasobanura neza ingene _ukwiyemeza_ gushirwa mu gisohoka canke mu mibumbe y'isoko rya Bitcoin, kugira ngo bimenyekane ko iyo Commitment ishobora gukurikiranywa no kugenzurwa.


#### Directed Acyclic Graph - DAG


DAG (canke *Acyclic Guided Graph*) ni igishushanyo kitagira inzinguzingu, gishoboza gutegura urutonde rw'ibintu. Ivyuma vy’amabara, nk’ibice _vy’amasezerano ya RGB, bishobora guserukirwa n’ama DAG.


Ku bindi bisobanuro: [Directed Acyclic Graph](Igishushanyo_c'Igishushanyo_C'Igishushanyo_C'Igishushanyo)


#### Gucapura


Gucapura ni urudodo rw’amakuru rwo guhitamwo abafise Contract bakurikirana bashobora kwinjira mu mateka ya Contract. Ico kintu kiriho, nk’akarorero, muri **RGB21** Interface kandi kiratuma amakuru y’icibutso canke y’insobanuro yongerwa ku mateka ya Contract.


#### Ikimenyamenya c'ibikorwa vy'inyongera - ETP


ETP (*Ikimenyamenya c'Ibikorwa vy'Iyongera*) ni igice ca Anchor kirimwo amakuru y'inyongera asabwa kugira ngo umuntu yemeze **Tapret** *Commitment* (mu bijanye na _taproot_). Harimwo, mu bindi, urufunguzo rwa bose rw'imbere rw'inyandiko ya Taproot (_internal PubKey_) n'amakuru yihariye ku _Inzira y'inyandiko Spend_.


#### Genesis


Genesis yerekeza ku rutonde rw'amakuru, ayoborwa na Schema, igize igihugu c'intango ca Contract iyo ari yo yose muri RGB. Bishobora kugereranywa n’iciyumviro ca Bitcoin ca _Genesis Block_, canke n’iciyumviro ca Coinbase Transaction, ariko hano ku rugero rwa _uruhande rw’umukiriya_ n’urwa RGB token.


#### Global State


Global State ni urutonde rw'ibintu vya bose biri muri Contract State. Isobanurwa kuri Genesis kandi, bivanye n’amategeko ya Contract, ishobora guhindurwa n’ihinduka ryemewe. Mu buryo butandukanye n’Ibihugu Bifise Ububasha, Global State ntabwo ari iy’ikigo kinaka; ni hafi cane y’inyandiko ya bose iri muri Contract.


#### Interface


Interface ni urutonde rw'amabwirizwa akoreshwa mu gusobanura amakuru abiri akoranijwe muri Schema canke mu bikorwa vya Contract n'imibereho yayo, kugira ngo ashobore gusomwa n'uwukoresha canke Wallet yiwe. Ikora nk'insobanuro Layer.


#### Interface Implementation


Interface Implementation ni umugwi w'amatangazo ahuza **Interface** na **Schema**. Bishoboza ubuhinduzi bw’insobanuro bukorwa na Interface ubwayo, kugira ngo amakuru atagiramwo ivyatsi yo muri Contract ashobore gutahurwa n’uwukoresha canke porogarama irimwo (amasakoshi).


#### Invoice


Invoice ifata uburyo bwa URL ishizwe muri [base58](https://ru.wikipedia.org/wiki/Binary-to-text encoding#Base58), ikaba ishiramwo amakuru akenewe kugira ngo umuntu yubake **State Transition** (n’uwuyitanga). Mu yandi majambo, ni Invoice ishoboza uwundi (*uwuriha*) gukora ihinduka rihuye n'iryo kugira ngo yimure umutungo canke avugurure uko Contract imeze.


#### Lightning Network


Lightning Network ni urubuga rwigenga rw’imihora yo kwishura (canke _imihora ya leta_) kuri Bitcoin, rugizwe n’ibipapuro 2/2 vy’imikono myinshi. Bishoboza gukora amafaranga yihuta, ataco atwara _inyuma y’uruzitiro_, mu gihe yizigira Layer 1 ya Bitcoin ku bijanye n’ubukemurampaka (canke gufunga) iyo bikenewe.


Kugira ngo umenye vyinshi ku buryo Lightning ikora, ndagusavye gufata iri shure rindi:


https://planb.network/courses/34bd43ef-6683-4a5c-b239-7cb1e40a4aeb

#### Multi Protocol Commitment - MPC


Multi Protocol Commitment (MPC) yerekeza ku miterere ya Merkle Tree ikoreshwa muri RGB kugira ngo ishiremwo, mu gikorwa kimwe ca Bitcoin, **Imigwi y’Impinduka** myinshi iva mu masezerano atandukanye. Iciyumviro ni ugushira hamwe amasezerano menshi (ashobora guhura n’amasezerano atandukanye canke itunga ritandukanye) mu ntumbero imwe ya Anchor kugira ngo umuntu ashobore gukoresha neza ikibanza c’amabuye.


#### Owned State


Owned State ni igice ca Contract State gipfutse muri Assignment kandi gifitaniye isano n’umuntu yihariye afise (biciye kuri Single-Use Seal yerekana UTXO). Ivyo bigereranya nk’akarorero umutungo wo kuri interineti canke uburenganzira bumwe bumwe bw’amasezerano uwo muntu yahawe.


#### Ownership


Ownership yerekeza ku bushobozi bwo kugenzura no gukoresha UTXO yerekanwa na Seal Definition. Iyo Owned State ifatanye na UTXO, nyen'iyo UTXO arafise uburenganzira, bishoboka, bwo kwimurira canke guhindura igihugu gifatanye, hakurikijwe amategeko ya Contract.


#### Partially Signed Bitcoin Transaction - PSBT


PSBT (_Igice ca Bitcoin gishizweko umukono_) ni igitabu ca Bitcoin kitarashirwako umukono ku buryo bushitse. Ishobora gusangizwa hagati y’ibigo vyinshi, kimwe cose kikaba gishobora kwongerako canke kugenzura Elements zimwe zimwe (imikono, inyandiko...), gushika iyo nzira y’ugucuruza ibonwa ko yiteguriye gukwiragizwa On-Chain.


Ku bindi bisobanuro: [BIP-0174] (BIP-0174.mediawiki)


#### Pedersen commitment


Pedersen commitment ni ubwoko bw'ibara ry'ibanga Commitment rifise akamaro ko kuba **homomorphic** ku bijanye n'igikorwa co kwongerako. Ivyo bisigura ko bishoboka kwemeza umubare w’imihigo ibiri ata guhishura agaciro k’umuntu ku giti ciwe.


Mu buryo busanzwe, nimba:


$$
C1=\text{commit}(m1,r1) \quad C2=\text{commit}(m2,r2)
$$


none:


$$
C3=C1⋅C2=\text{commit}(m1+m2, r1+r2)
$$


Iyi nzira ni ngirakamaro, nk'akarorero, mu guhisha amafaranga y'ibimenyetso vyahinduwe, mu gihe ushobora kugenzura igitigiri cose.


Ibindi bisobanuro: [Pedersen commitment] (igice ca 10.1007/3-540-46766-1_9)


#### Redeem


Mu State Extension, Redeem yerekeza ku gikorwa co gusubira gusaba (canke gukoresha nabi) **Valency** yari yatangajwe mbere. Kubera ko Valency ari uburenganzira bwa bose, Redeem iremeza uwufise uburenganzira bwo gusaba Contract State Extension yihariye.


#### Schema


Schema muri RGB ni igice c'itangazo ry'itegeko ridondora urutonde rw'ibihinduka, amategeko na Business Logic (*Business Logic*) bigenzura ibikorwa vya Contract. Schema isobanura imiterere ya Leta, ubwoko bw’ihinduka ryemewe n’ivyo kwemeza.


#### Seal Definition


Seal Definition ni igice ca Assignment gifatanya _ukwiyemeza_ na UTXO y'uwuyifise mushasha. Mu yandi majambo, yerekana aho ivyangombwa biri (aho UTXO iri), kandi igashinga Ownership y’umutungo canke uburenganzira.


#### Shard


Shard igereranya ishami muri DAG y'amateka y'Impinduka za Leta ya RGB Contract. Mu yandi majambo, ni igice gihuye c'amateka yose ya Contract, gihuye, nk'akarorero, n'urutonde rw'ibintu bisabwa kugira ngo umuntu yerekane ko umutungo kanaka ufise ukuri kuva mu _Itanguriro_.


#### Single-Use Seal


Single-Use Seal ni umuhango w’ibanga wa Commitment ku butumwa butaramenyekana, buzohishurirwa rimwe gusa muri kazoza kandi butegerezwa kumenyekana n’abagize umuryango w’abantu bose. Intumbero ni ukubuza gushinga amasezerano menshi y'uguhiganwa ku Seal imwe.


#### Stash


Stash ni urutonde rw’amakuru y’uruhande rw’umukiriya umukoresha abika ku masezerano imwe canke menshi ya RGB, kugira ngo yemezwe (*Client-side Validation*). Ivyo birimwo amateka y’ihinduka, ivy’ugurungika, ibimenyamenya vy’ukuri, n’ibindi.Umuntu wese afise aguma afise gusa ibice vy’amateka akeneye (*shards*).


#### State Extension


State Extension ni Contract Operation ikoreshwa mu gusubira gutera ivyagezwe vya leta mu gucungura **Ivy'agaciro** vyamenyeshejwe mbere. Kugira ngo State Extension ikore neza, itegerezwa rero gupfungwa na State Transition (ihindura uko Contract imeze).


#### State Transition


State Transition ni igikorwa gihindura ikibanza ca RGB Contract kikaja mu kibanza gishasha. Ishobora guhindura amakuru ya Global State na/canke Owned State. Mu bikorwa, uguhinduka kwose kugenzurwa n'amategeko ya Schema kandi gushirwa mu Bitcoin Blockchain biciye ku _ukwiyemeza_.


#### Taproot


Ivuga ku buryo bwo gukoresha Bitcoin bwa SegWit v1, bwashizweho na [BIP341] [BIP342] (Ubuhinga bwo gusoma amakuru). Taproot itera imbere ibanga n’uguhinduranya inyandiko, cane cane mu gutuma amafaranga akoreshwa akora neza kandi akagora gutandukanya n’ayandi.


#### Terminal Consignment - Consignment Endpoint


Terminal Consignment (canke _Iherezo ry’Ibirungikwa_) ni *Consignment yo kwimurira* irimwo ivy’iherezo vya Contract, harimwo na State Transition yaremwe ivuye kuri Invoice y’uwuyironka (*uwuhembwa*). Ni co rero gisozera ukwimurirwa, harimwo amakuru akenewe kugira ngo yerekane ko Ownership canke leta yimuriwe.


#### Transition Bundle


Transition Bundle ni umugwi w'Impinduka za Leta (ziri muri Contract imwe) zose zikora ***Witness Transaction*** Bitcoin imwe. Ivyo bituma bishoboka gukoranya ibintu vyinshi bishasha canke kwimurirwa muri On-Chain Anchor imwe.


#### UTXO


Bitcoin UTXO (*Igisubizo c’Ibikorwa Bitakoreshejwe*) isobanurwa na Hash y’ibikorwa n’urutonde rw’ibikorwa (*vout*). Rimwe na rimwe ryitwa kandi _isonga_. Mu masezerano ya RGB, kwerekeza kuri UTXO (biciye kuri **Seal Definition**) bishoboza aho **Owned State** iri, ni ukuvuga umutungo ufise kuri Blockchain.


#### Valency


Valency ni uburenganzira bwa bose budasaba ububiko bwa Leta nk'uko buri, ariko bushobora gucungurwa biciye ku **State Extension**. Ni uburyo rero bw’ubushobozi bufunguriye bose (canke abakinyi bamwebamwe), bumenyeshwa mu nzira y’ubwenge ya Contract, kugira ngo hakorwe ukwongerekana kw’igihe kinaka mu nyuma.


#### Witness Transaction


Witness Transaction ni igikorwa ca Bitcoin gifunga Single-Use Seal gikikuje ubutumwa burimwo Multi Protocol Commitment (MPC). Ivyo bicuruzwa bikoresha UTXO canke bikabirema, kugira ngo Seal Commitment ihuye n’umurongo wa RGB. Ikora nk’ikimenyamenya ca On-Chain c’uko Leta yashizweho mu gihe kinaka.


# Porogaramu kuri RGB


<partId>148a7436-d079-56d9-be08-aaa4c14c6b3a</partId>


## Gushira mu ngiro amasezerano ya RGB


<chapterId>8333ea5f-51c7-5dd5-b1d7-47d491e58e51</chapterId>


:::id ya videwo=97d81b85-5a82-40a5-b111-7d96be5afd0f:::


Muri iki gice, turaza kuraba neza ingene RGB Contract isobanurwa kandi igashirwa mu ngiro. Turabona ibice bigize RGB Contract ni ibiki, uruhara rwavyo n’ingene vyubatswe.


### Ibice vy'indege ya RGB Contract


Kugeza ubu, twamaze kuvuga kuri **Genesis**, igereranya intango ya Contract, kandi twabonye ingene ihuye n'ubwenge bwa *Contract Operation* n'ingene protocole iri. Insobanuro yuzuye ya RGB Contract, ariko, ntigarukira kuri Genesis yonyene: irimwo ibice bitatu vyuzuzanya, vyose hamwe, bikaba bigize umutima w’ugushirwa mu ngiro.


Igice ca mbere citwa **Schema**. Iyi ni dosiye idondora imiterere y'ishimikiro na Business Logic (*Business Logic*) ya Contract. Irasobanura ubwoko bw’amakuru akoreshwa, amategeko yo kwemeza, ibikorwa vyemewe (nk’ugutanga token mu ntango, ukwimurira, ivyangombwa bidasanzwe, n’ibindi) - muri make, inzego rusangi zitegeka ingene Contract ikora.


Igice ca kabiri ni **Interface**. Bishimikiye cane ku kuntu abakoresha (kandi mu kwagura, porogaramu y'ibikorwa) bazokorana n'iyi Contract. Iradondora insobanuro, ni ukuvuga uguserukira gusomwa kw’ibice bitandukanye n’ibikorwa. Rero, mu gihe Schema isobanura ingene Contract ikora mu buryo bw’ubuhinga, Interface isobanura ingene yoshikiriza no gushikiriza ivyo bikoresho: amazina y’uburyo, kwerekana amakuru, n’ibindi.


Igice ca gatatu ni **Interface Implementation**, kikaba kizuza ibindi bibiri vyabanje mu gukora nk'ikiraro hagati ya Schema na Interface. Mu yandi majambo, rifatanya insobanuro yerekanwa na Interface n’amategeko ashingiyeko asobanuwe muri Schema. Iryo shirwa mu ngiro ni ryo rizocungera, nk’akarorero, uguhindura hagati y’umurongo winjijwe muri Wallet n’imiterere y’ibice bibiri itegekanijwe n’umurongo, canke gukoranya amategeko y’ukwemeza mu rurimi rw’imashini.


Ubwo buhinga ni ikintu gishimishije muri RGB, kuko butuma imigwi itandukanye y’abahinguzi bakora ukwabo kuri ivyo bintu (*Schema*, *Interface*, *Ishirwa mu ngiro*), igihe cose bakurikije amategeko y’uguhurizako y’amasezerano.


Mu guca irya n’ino, Contract yose igizwe na:




- **Genesis**, ​​ari ryo ry'intango rya Contract (kandi rishobora kugereranywa n'ugucuruza kudasanzwe gusobanura Ownership ya mbere y'umutungo, uburenganzira, canke ayandi makuru yose ashobora guhindurwa);
- **Schema**, idondora Business Logic ya Contract (ubwoko bw'amakuru, amategeko yo kwemeza, n'ibindi);
- **Interface**, itanga insobanuro Layer ku bikoresho vyompi n'abakoresha abantu, isobanura ugusoma n'ugushirwa mu ngiro kw'ibikorwa;
- Ishirwa mu ngiro **Interface**, igabanya ikinogo kiri hagati ya Business Logic n'ugushikiriza, kugira ngo insobanuro ya Contract ihure n'ubumenyi bw'ukoresha.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/070.webp)


Ni ngombwa kumenya ko kugira ngo Wallet ishobore gucunga umutungo wa RGB (yaba token ishobora guhindurwa canke uburenganzira bw’ubwoko bwose), itegerezwa kuba ifise izo Elements zose zikoranijwe: *Schema*, *Interface*, *GW-134*35. Ivyo birungikwa biciye ku ***Contract Consignment***, ni ukuvuga amakuru arimwo vyose bikenewe kugira ngo wemeze Contract y'umukiriya.


Kugira ngo dufashe gusobanura ivyo vyiyumviro, ng’iyi imbonerahamwe y’incamake igereranya ibice vya RGB Contract n’ivyiyumviro bimaze kumenyekana haba mu gukora porogarama zishingiye ku bintu (OOP) canke mu bidukikije vya Ethereum:


| RGB Contract Component       | Meaning                        | OOP Equivalent                                     | Ethereum Equivalent                |
| ---------------------------- | ------------------------------ | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------- |
| **Genesis**                  | Initial state of the contract  | Class constructor                                  | Contract constructor               |
| **Schema**                   | Business logic of the contract | Class                                              | Contract                           |
| **Interface**                | Semantics of the contract      | Interface (Java) / Trait (Rust) / Protocol (Swift) | ERC Standard                       |
| **Interface Implementation** | Mapping semantics and logic    | Impl (Rust) / Implements (Java)                    | Application Binary Interface (ABI) |


Inkingi y’ibubamfu yerekana Elements yihariye ku bijanye n’umurongo wa RGB. Inkingi yo hagati yerekana igikorwa nyaco c’igice kimwekimwe cose. Hanyuma, mu nkingi ya "OOP equivalent", dusanga ijambo ringana muri porogarama zishingiye ku kintu:




- **Genesis** ifise uruhara rusa n'urw'umuhinguzi w'Ikigo: niho igihugu ca Contract gitangura;
- **Schema** ni insobanuro y’umugwi, ni ukuvuga insobanuro y’imiterere yawo, uburyo bwawo n’intumbero yawo;
- **Interface** ihuye n' *ibimenyetso* (Java), *ibiranga* (Rust) canke *amasezerano* (Swift): ivyo ni vyo bisobanuro vya bose vy'ibikorwa, ibintu, imirima...;
- **Interface Implementation** ihuye na *Impl* muri Rust canke *Implements* muri Java, aho dusobanura ingene kode izokora uburyo bwamenyeshejwe muri Interface.


Mu bijanye n'ivy'ubuhinga bwa Ethereum, Genesis iri hafi cane y'umwubatsi wa **Contract**, Schema iri hafi y'insobanuro ya Contract, Interface iri hafi y'urugero nka ERC-20 canke ERC-721, na Interface Implementation iri hafi y'insobanuro ya **ABI**, uburyo bwo gukorana na Contract.


Inyungu y’uko RGB ishobora gukoreshwa mu buryo bw’ibice (modularité) na yo iri mu kuba abafatanyabikorwa batandukanye bashobora kwandika, nk’akarorero, Interface Implementation yabo, igihe cose bubaha ubusobanuro bwa *Schema* n’insobanuro ya *Interface*. Gutyo, uwutanga amakuru yoshobora gutegura imbere nshasha, ikoreshwa neza cane (Interface), ataco ahinduye ku nsiguro ya Contract, canke ibihushanye n’ivyo, umuntu yoshobora kwagura Schema kugira ngo yongereko ibikorwa, maze agatanga verisiyo nshasha y’ibikorwa vy’ishimikiro vya Interface Implementation vyahinduwe, mu gihe ibikorwa vya kera vy’ishimikiro vyogumaho.


Iyo dukoranye Contract nshasha, dukora Genesis (intambwe ya mbere yo gutanga canke gutanga umutungo), hamwe n’ibigize (Schema, Interface, Interface Implementation). Inyuma y’ivyo, Contract irakora neza kandi irashobora gukwiragizwa ku ma wallets no ku bakoresha. Ubu buryo, aho Genesis ifatanijwe n’ivyo bice bitatu, butanga icemezo c’urugero rwo hejuru rw’uguhindura (buri Contract ishobora kugira ivyiyumviro vyayo), kwegereza ubutegetsi (umuntu wese ashobora gutanga umusanzu ku gice kinaka), n’umutekano (ugushingira intahe biguma bisobanuwe cane n’umurongo w’amategeko, ata gushingira ku arbitry onG on8- izindi nzira z’amabuye).


Ubu rero ndashaka kwihweza neza kimwe cose muri ivyo bice: **Schema**, **Interface** na **Interface Implementation**.


### Schema


Mu gice ca mbere, twabonye ko mu bidukikije vya RGB, Contract igizwe n’ibidukikije vyinshi: Genesis, bishinga intahe ivy’intango, n’ibindi bihimba vyinshi vy’inyongera. Intumbero ya Schema ni ugusobanura neza Business Logic yose ya Contract, ni ukuvuga imiterere y’amakuru, ubwoko bukoreshwa, ibikorwa vyemewe n’ingene bimeze. Ni ikintu gihambaye cane rero mu gutuma Contract ikora ku ruhande rw’umukiriya, kuko uwuriko arayigiramwo wese (Wallet, nk’akarorero) ategerezwa kugenzura ko amahinduka ya leta aronka ahuye n’ubwenge busobanuwe muri Schema.


Schema ishobora kugereranywa n'"umugwi" mu gukora porogarama zishingiye ku bintu (OOP). Muri rusangi, ikora nk’akarorero gasobanura ibice bigize Contract, nk’akarorero:




- Ubwoko butandukanye bw’Ibihugu vy’Igihugu n’Ibikorwa;
- Valencies, ni ukuvuga uburenganzira budasanzwe bushobora guterwa (*gucungurwa*) ku bikorwa bimwebimwe;
- Global State, zidondora ivy’isi yose, ivy’abantu bose n’ivy’abantu bose vya Contract;
- Igishushanyo ca Genesis (igikorwa ca mbere nyene gikora Contract);
- Uburyo bwemewe bw’Impinduka za Leta n’Ivyaguwe vya Leta, n’ingene ivyo bikorwa bishobora guhindura;
- Metadata ijana n’igikorwa cose, kugira ngo ubike amakuru y’igihe gito canke y’inyongera;
- Amategeko agena ingene amakuru yo mu mutima ya Contract ashobora gutera imbere (nk’akarorero, nimba umurima ushobora guhinduka canke ushobora kwirundanira);
- Urutonde rw’ibikorwa bibonwa ko bifise akamaro: nk’akarorero, urutonde rw’ihinduka ry’ibintu ryubahirizwa canke urutonde rw’ibintu bihuye n’ubwenge bikwiye gushitswako.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/071.webp)


Iyo *uwutanga* umutungo uri kuri RGB asohoye Contract, atanga Genesis na Schema zijana na wo. Abakoresha canke ama wallet bipfuza gukorana n’itunga bararonka iyi Schema kugira ngo batahure ivyiyumviro biri inyuma ya Contract, no kugira ngo bashobore kugenzura mu nyuma ko amahinduka bazogiramwo uruhara ari ay’ukuri.


Intambwe ya mbere, ku muntu wese aronka amakuru yerekeye umutungo wa RGB (nk'akarorero, ukwimurira token), ni ukwemeza ayo makuru ku Schema. Ivyo birimwo gukoresha igitabu Schema kugira ngo:




- Suzuma ko Ibihugu vy’Umutungo, Ibikorwa n’ibindi Elements bisobanuwe neza kandi ko vyubahiriza ubwoko bwategetswe (ivyo bita *strict type system*);
- Suzuma ko amategeko y’uguhindura (inyandiko zo kwemeza) yuzuye. Izo nyandiko zishobora gukoreshwa biciye ku AluVM, iri ku ruhande rw’umukiriya kandi ishinzwe kwemeza ko Business Logic ihuye (amahera yoherezwa, ivyangombwa bidasanzwe, n’ibindi).


Mu bikorwa, Schema si kode ishobora gukorwa, nk’uko bishobora kubonwa mu ma blockchain abika ku-chain code (EVM kuri Ethereum). Ahubwo, RGB itandukanya Business Logic (itangazo) na kode ishobora gushirwa mu ngiro kuri Blockchain (iyigarukira ku nzitizi z’ubuhinga). Gutyo, Schema ni yo igena amategeko, ariko ugushira mu ngiro ayo mategeko bibera hanze ya Blockchain, ku kibanza c’uwuje mu nama wese, hakurikijwe ingingo ngenderwako ya Client-side Validation.


Schema itegerezwa gukoranirizwa imbere y’uko ikoreshwa n’ibikorwa vya RGB. Iyi nkuru itanga dosiye y'ibice bibiri (nk'akarorero `.RGB`) canke dosiye y'ibice bibiri (`.rgba`). Iyo Wallet yinjije iyi dosiye, iramenya:




- Ivyo ubwoko bumwe bumwe bw’amakuru (imibare yose, imiterere, imirongo...) busa kubera uburyo bw’ubwoko bukomeye;
- Uko Genesis ikwiye gutunganirizwa (kugira ngo umuntu atahure intango y’itunga);
- Ubwoko butandukanye bw’ibikorwa (Impinduka za Leta, Ukwagura Leta) n’ingene bishobora guhindura Leta;
- Amategeko y’inyandiko (yashizwe muri Schema) moteri ya AluVM izokoresha kugira ngo isuzume ko ibikorwa bifise ukuri.


Nk’uko vyasiguwe mu bice vyabanje, *uburyo bw’ubwoko bukomeye* buraduha uburyo bwo gushiramwo amakuru buhamye, bushingiye ku vyo umuntu abona: ibihinduka vyose, vyaba Ibihugu vy’Umutungo, Ibihugu vy’Isi yose canke Ivy’Uburemere, biradondaguwe neza (ubunini, imbibe zo hasi n’izo hejuru nimba bikenewe, ubwoko bufise umukono canke butashizweko umukono, n’ibindi). Birashoboka kandi gusobanura imiterere y'ivyatsi, nk'akarorero gushigikira ibibazo vy'ikoreshwa bikomeye.


Mu buryo bw'ubushake, Schema ishobora gukoresha umuzi `SchemaId`, bifasha gusubira gukoresha imiterere y'ishimikiro iriho (ikigereranyo). Muri ubu buryo, ushobora guhindura Contract canke guhingura ibintu bihinduka (nk'ubwoko bushasha bwa token) uhereye ku citegererezo camaze kwemezwa. Ukwo guhinduranya amasezerano kurarinda gusubira gukora amasezerano yose, kandi kuraremesha uguhuza ingendo nziza.


Ikindi kintu gihambaye ni uko ubuhinga bwo gutera imbere kwa Leta (uguhindura, guhindura, n’ibindi) budondora muri Schema mu buryo bw’inyandiko, amategeko n’ivyangombwa. Rero, nimba umuhinguzi wa Contract yipfuza kwemerera gusubira gusohoka canke gushinga uburyo bwo guturira (ugusambura ibimenyetso), arashobora gusobanura inyandiko zihuye na AluVM mu gice co kwemeza Schema.


#### Itandukaniro n'ibindi bishobora gukorwa On-Chain


Udakunze ubuhinga nka Ethereum, aho kode ya Smart contract (ishobora gukorwa) yandikwa muri Blockchain ubwayo, RGB ibika Contract (ubwenge bwayo) off-chain, mu buryo bw’inyandiko y’imenyekanisha ikoranijwe. Ivyo bisigura ko:




- Nta VM yuzuye ya Turing ikora mu nzira yose y’urubuga rwa Bitcoin. Amategeko ya RGB Contract ntashirwa mu ngiro kuri Blockchain, ariko mu mukoresha wese yipfuza kwemeza Leta;
- Amakuru ya Contract ntahumanya Blockchain: ibimenyamenya vy’ubuhinga bwo gukingira amakuru (*ivyemezo*) vyonyene ni vyo bishirwa mu bikorwa vya Bitcoin (biciye muri `Tapret` canke `Opret`);
- Schema ishobora guhindurwa canke igakurwako (*kwihuta-imbere*, *gusunika-inyuma*, n'ibindi), ataco bisaba Fork kuri Bitcoin Blockchain. Amasakoshi akeneye gusa kwinjiza mu gihugu Schema nshasha no kumenyera amahinduka y’ubumwe.


#### Ikoreshwa n'uwutanga n'abakoresha


Iyo *umutanga* aremye umutungo (nk’akarorero, token idashobora guhinduka), ategura:




- Igitabo ca Schema kidondora amategeko agenga ivy’ugusohora, uguhindura n’ibindi;
- Genesis ihuye n’iyi Schema (irimwo umubare wose w’ibimenyetso vyasohowe, akaranga ka nyen’ivyo bimenyetso vya mbere, Valencies zidasanzwe zo gusubira gusohoka, n’ibindi).


Ica ituma Schema (dosiye `.RGB`) yashizwe hamwe iboneka ku bakoresha, kugira ngo umuntu wese yaronse ubutumwa bwo muri iyo token ashobore kugenzura ukuntu igikorwa gihuye mu karere. Iyo ata Schema, uwuyikoresha ntiyoshobora gusobanura amakuru y’ivy’imimerere canke ngo asuzume ko yubahiriza amategeko ya Contract.


Rero iyo Wallet nshasha ishaka gushigikira umutungo, ikeneye gusa gushiramwo Schema ibereye. Ubu buryo buratuma bishoboka kwongerako uguhuza ku bwoko bushasha bw’itunga rya RGB, ata guhindura mu buryo buteye ubwoba urufatiro rwa porogarama ya Wallet: ibisabwa vyose ni ukuzana mu gihugu Schema binary no gutahura imiterere yayo.


Schema isobanura Business Logic muri RGB.
