Iratanga urutonde rw’amategeko y’iterambere ry’igikoresho ca Contract, imiterere y’amakuru yaco (Ibihugu vy’ubutunzi, Global State, Ivyiyumviro vy’agaciro) n’inyandiko z’ukwemeza zijana (zishobora gukorwa na AluVM). Kubera iyi nyandiko y’itangazo, insobanuro ya Contract (dosiye ikoranijwe) itandukanye neza n’ugushirwa mu ngiro nyakuri kw’amategeko (uruhande rw’umukiriya). Ivyo bituma RGB ishobora guhindura cane, bikaba bishoboza gukoresha ibintu vyinshi (ibimenyetso bishobora guhinduka, NFT, amasezerano ateye igomwe) mu gihe yirinda ugusobanuka n’amakosa asanzwe mu bikoresho vya On-Chain bishobora gutegurwa.


#### Akarorero ka Schema


Reka turabe akarorero nyako ka Schema ku RGB Contract. Iyi ni igice kiri muri Rust muri dosiye `nia.rs` (inyuguti z'intango za "*Itunga Ridashobora Gukura*"), risobanura akarorero k'ibimenyetso bishobora guhinduka bidashobora gusubira gusohoka birenze Supply yabo ya mbere (itunga ridashobora gutera). Ubwo bwoko bwa token bushobora kubonwa nk’ubungana, mu gisata ca RGB, bwa ERC20 kuri Ethereum, ni ukuvuga ibimenyetso bishobora guhinduka vyubahiriza amategeko amwe amwe y’ishimikiro (nk’akarorero ku kwimurira, gutangura Supply, n’ibindi).


Imbere yo kwisuka muri kode, birabereye kwibuka imiterere rusangi ya RGB Schema. Hari urutonde rw'amatangazo ashinzwe:




- `SchemaId` ishoboka yerekana ikoreshwa ry'iyindi Schema y'ishimikiro nk'akarorero;
- **Ibihugu vy’Isi yose** na **Ibihugu vy’Igihugu** (n’ubwoko bwavyo bukomeye);
- **Ivyiza** (niba biriho);
- Ivyo **Ibikorwa** (Genesis, Impinduka za Leta, Ukwaguka kw’Igihugu) bishobora kwerekeza kuri ivyo bihugu n’ivyo bihugu;
- **Ubwoko bukomeye** bukoreshwa mu kudondora no kwemeza amakuru;
- **Ivyanditswe vyemeza** (bikoreshwa biciye kuri AluVM).


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/072.webp)


Kode iri musi yerekana insobanuro yuzuye ya Rust Schema. Tuzobivuga igice ku kindi, dukurikije ibisobanuro (1) gushika kuri (9) biri aha hepfo:


```rust
// ===== PART 1: Function Header and SubSchema =====
fn nia_schema() -> SubSchema {

// definitions of libraries and variables

// ===== PART 2: General Properties (ffv, subset_of, type_system) =====
Schema {
ffv: zero!(),
subset_of: None,
type_system: types.type_system(),

// ===== PART 3: Global States =====
global_types: tiny_bmap! {
GS_NOMINAL => GlobalStateSchema::once(types.get("RGBContract.DivisibleAssetSpec")),
GS_DATA => GlobalStateSchema::once(types.get("RGBContract.ContractData")),
GS_TIMESTAMP => GlobalStateSchema::once(types.get("RGBContract.Timestamp")),
GS_ISSUED_SUPPLY => GlobalStateSchema::once(types.get("RGBContract.Amount")),
},

// ===== PART 4: Owned Types =====
owned_types: tiny_bmap! {
OS_ASSET => StateSchema::Fungible(FungibleType::Unsigned64Bit),
},

// ===== PART 5: Valencies =====
valency_types: none!(),

// ===== PART 6: Genesis: Initial Operations =====
genesis: GenesisSchema {
metadata: Ty::<SemId>::UNIT.id(None),
globals: tiny_bmap! {
GS_NOMINAL => Occurrences::Once,
GS_DATA => Occurrences::Once,
GS_TIMESTAMP => Occurrences::Once,
GS_ISSUED_SUPPLY => Occurrences::Once,
},
assignments: tiny_bmap! {
OS_ASSET => Occurrences::OnceOrMore,
},
valencies: none!(),
},

// ===== PART 7: Extensions =====
extensions: none!(),

// ===== PART 8: Transitions: TS_TRANSFER =====
transitions: tiny_bmap! {
TS_TRANSFER => TransitionSchema {
metadata: Ty::<SemId>::UNIT.id(None),
globals: none!(),
inputs: tiny_bmap! {
OS_ASSET => Occurrences::OnceOrMore,
},
assignments: tiny_bmap! {
OS_ASSET => Occurrences::OnceOrMore,
},
valencies: none!(),
}
},

// ===== PART 9: Script AluVM and Entry Points =====
script: Script::AluVM(AluScript {
libs: confined_bmap! { alu_id => alu_lib },
entry_points: confined_bmap! {
EntryPoint::ValidateGenesis => LibSite::with(FN_GENESIS_OFFSET, alu_id),
EntryPoint::ValidateTransition(TS_TRANSFER) => LibSite::with(FN_TRANSFER_OFFSET, alu_id),
},
}),
}
}
```




- (1) - **Umutwe w'ibikorwa n'Igishushanyo**


`nia_schema()` igikorwa kigarura `Igishushanyo gito`, kigaragaza ko iyi Schema ishobora kuragwa igice ca Schema rusangi. Mu bidukikije vya RGB, ukwo guhinduranya gutuma bishoboka gusubira gukoresha Elements imwe imwe y’umukuru Schema, hanyuma ugasobanura amategeko yihariye kuri Contract iriko iravugwa. Aha, duhitamwo kudashoboza iragi, kuko `subset_of` izoba `Nta`.




- (2) - Ibirango rusangi: ffv, igice_c', **ubwoko_bw'uburyo**


Igikoresho ca `ffv` gihuye n'ivyo *vyihuta* vya Contract. Agaciro ka `zero!()` hano kerekana ko turi kuri verisiyo 0 canke verisiyo ya mbere y'iyi Schema. Niba mu nyuma wipfuza kwongerako ibikorwa bishasha (ubwoko bushasha bw'ibikorwa, n'ibindi), ushobora kwongera iyi verisiyo kugira ngo werekane ihinduka ry'ukwemeranya.


I `subset_of: Nta` umutungo wemeza ko ata n'iragi. `ubwoko_uburyo` umwanya werekeye ubwoko bukomeye bwa sisitemu busanzwe busobanuwe mu `ubwoko` ububiko bw'ibitabo. Uyu murongo werekana ko amakuru yose akoreshwa na Contract akoresha ugushirwa mu ngiro kw’urutonde gukomeye gutangwa n’ububiko bw’ibitabu buvugwa.




- (3) - Ibihugu vyo kw'isi yose


Mu `ubwoko_bw'isi yose`, dutangaza Elements zine. Dukoresha urufunguzo, nka `GS_IZINA` canke `GS_ISOHOKA_ITANGA`, kugira ngo tubikoreshe mu nyuma:




- `GS_NOMINAL` yerekeza ku bwoko bwa `DivisibleAssetSpec`, budondora ivyicaro bitandukanye vya token yaremwe (izina ryose, ikimenyetso, ukuri...);
- `GS_DATA` igereranya amakuru rusangi, nk'ukwiyamiriza, amakuru y'imbere, canke uwundi munyandiko;
- `GS_TIMESTAMP` yerekana itariki y'isohoka;
- `GS_ISSUED_SUPPLY` ishiraho umubare wose Supply, ni ukuvuga umubare munini w'ibimenyetso bishobora kuremwa.


Ijambo ry'ingenzi `rimwe(...)` risobanura ko buri kimwe muri ivyo bibanza gishobora kugaragara rimwe gusa.




- (4) - Ubwoko bw'ibintu


Mu `ubwoko_bufise`, dutangaza `OS_ASSET`, idondora igihugu gishobora guhinduka. Dukoresha `StateSchema::Fungible(Ubwoko::Unsigned64Bit)`, vyerekana ko umubare w'itunga (ibimenyetso) ubitswe nk'umubare wose udashizweko umukono w'ibice 64. Gutyo, igikorwa cose kizorungika umubare kanaka w’ibice vy’iyi token, ivyo bikaba bizokwemezwa hakurikijwe iyo mibare yanditswe neza.




- (5) - **Ivyiza**


Twerekana `valency_types: none!()`, bisobanura ko ata Valencies ziri muri iyi Schema, mu yandi majambo nta burenganzira budasanzwe canke bwongerekanye (nk'ugusubira gusohora, guturira bitegekanijwe, n'ibindi). Iyo Schema irimwo ivyo, vyomenyeshwa muri iki gice.




- (6) - Genesis: ibikorwa vya mbere


Aha twinjira mu gice kimenyesha Ibikorwa vya Contract. Genesis idondorwa na:




- Kubura `amakuru y'imbere` (umurima `amakuru y'imbere: Ty::<SemId>::UNIT.id(Nta)`);
- Ibihugu vyo kw’isi yose bitegerezwa kubaho rimwe kuri kimwe cose (`Rimwe`);
- Urutonde rw'ibikorwa aho `OS_ASSET` itegerezwa kugaragara `RimweCanke N'ibindi`. Ivyo bisigura ko Genesis isaba nibura `OS_ASSET` imwe Assignment (uwuyifise mu ntango);
- Oya Valency: `ubushobozi: nta n'umwe!()`.


Uko ni ko duca ku rugero rw'insobanuro y'ikibazo ca mbere ca token: dutegerezwa kumenyesha Supply yasohowe (`GS_ISSUED_SUPPLY`), twongereko n'imiburiburi uwuyifise (Owned State y'ubwoko `OS_ASSET`).




- (7) - Ukwagura


`Ivyagutse: nta!()` vyerekana ko ata State Extension itegekanijwe muri iyi Contract. Ivyo bisigura ko ata gikorwa co gukora Redeem uburenganzira bwa digitale (Valency) canke gukora State Extension imbere y’Impinduka. Ivyo vyose bikorwa biciye ku Genesis canke ku nzira za Leta.




- (8) - Impinduka: TS_GUHINDURA


Mu `mihindukire`, dusobanura `TS_TRANSFER` ubwoko bw'igikorwa. Turasigura ko:




- Nta nkuru y’imbere ifise;
- Ntihindura Global State (ivyo bikaba vyaramaze gusobanurwa muri Genesis);
- Bifata `OS_ASSETs` imwe canke nyinshi nk'ivyo kwinjiza. Ivyo bisigura ko itegerezwa gukoresha Leta Zifise Ubutunzi zisanzweho;
- Irema (`ibikorwa`) nibura `OS_ASSET` imwe nshasha (mu yandi majambo, uwuronka canke abaronka baronka ibimenyetso);
- Nta Valency nshasha itanga.


Ivyo bigereranya inyifato y’ukwimurira kw’ishimikiro, gufungura ibimenyetso kuri UTXO, hanyuma bikarema Leta nshasha zifise ububasha ku neza y’abaronka, gutyo bikazigama uburinganire bw’amahera yose hagati y’ivyo yinjiza n’ivyo isohoka.




- (9) - **Inyandiko ya AluVM n'Ivyiyumviro vy'Injira** (mu gifaransa)


Ubwa nyuma, dutangaza inyandiko ya AluVM (`Inyandiko::AluVM(Inyandiko ya Alu { ... })`). Iyi nyandiko irimwo:




- Isoko rimwe canke menshi ry'inyuma (`libs`) rizokoreshwa mu gihe co kwemeza;
- Ivyinjira vyerekana ibikorwa bihinduka muri kode ya AluVM, bihuye n'ukwemeza kwa Genesis (`Kwemeza Itanguriro`) na buri mpinduka yatangajwe (`KwemezaImpinduka(TS_TRANSFER)`).


Iyi kode y'ukwemeza ni yo ishinzwe gukoresha Business Logic. Nk'akarorero, izosuzuma:




- Ko `GS_ISOHOKA_IBIMENYETSO` itarenze mu gihe ca Genesis;
- Ko umubare w'ibintu vyinjijwe` (ibimenyetso vyakoreshejwe) ungana n'umubare w'ibikorwa` (ibimenyetso vyakiriwe) ku `TS_TRANSFER`.


Iyo ayo mategeko atubahirijwe, iyo mpinduka izobonwa ko ata co imaze.


Aka karorero k'"*Itunga Ridashobora Gufutwa*" Schema karaduha ugutahura neza imiterere y'Itunga ryoroshe RGB token Contract. Turashobora kubona neza itandukaniro riri hagati y’insobanuro y’amakuru (Ibihugu vy’Isi yose n’Ibihugu vy’Igihugu), itangazo ry’ibikorwa (Genesis, Impinduka, Ukwagura) n’ugushirwa mu ngiro kw’ivyemezo (inyandiko za AluVM). Kubera iki kigereranyo, token yitwararika nk’iyitwa token, ariko iguma yemejwe ku ruhande rw’umukiriya kandi ntiyivana n’ibikorwa remezo vya On-Chain kugira ngo ikore kode yayo. Ivyemezo vy'ubuhinga bwo gukingira amakuru ni vyo vyonyene bishingiye kuri Bitcoin Blockchain.


### Interface


Interface ni Layer yagenewe gutuma Contract isomwa kandi ikoreshwa, n’abayikoresha (ugusoma kw’abantu) be n’ibitabo (ugusoma kwa porogarama). Interface rero irafise uruhara rugereranywa n’urw’i Interface mu rurimi rw’iporogarama rushingiye ku bintu (Java, akaranga ka Rust, n’ibindi), kuko igaragaza kandi igasobanura neza imiterere y’imikorere ya Contract, ataco isobanura ku bijanye n’ivyo Contract ikora.


Udakunze Schema, ivuga gusa kandi ikoranijwe muri dosiye y’ibice bibiri igoye gukoresha uko iri, Interface itanga imfunguruzo zo gusoma zikenewe kugira ngo:




- Gutanga urutonde no gusobanura Ibihugu vyo kw’Isi yose n’Ibihugu vy’Igihugu biri muri Contract;
- Ushobora gushika ku mazina n’agaciro k’umwanya wose, kugira ngo bishobore kwerekanwa (nk’akarorero ku token, umenye igiharuro cawo, umubare munini, n’ibindi);
- Gusobanura no kwubaka Ibikorwa vya Contract (Genesis, State Transition, canke State Extension) mu gufatanya amakuru n'amazina atahurwa (nk'akarorero, gukora ukwimurira mu gusobanura neza "umubare" aho gukoresha ikimenyetso c'ibice bibiri).


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/073.webp)


Ushimira Interface, urashobora, nk'akarorero, kwandika kode muri Wallet iyo, aho gukoresha ivyatsi, ikoresha ataco ihinduye ibimenyetso nk'"umubare w'ibimenyetso", "izina ry'umutungo", n'ibindi. Muri ubwo buryo, uburongozi bwa Contract burarushiriza kuba ubw’agaciro.


#### Ibikorwa rusangi


Ubwo buryo burafise ivyiza vyinshi:




- Gushinga urugero:


Ubwo bwoko bumwe bwa Contract burashobora gushigikirwa na Interface isanzwe, isangiwe hagati y'ibikorwa vyinshi vya Wallet. Ivyo bituma vyoroha guhuza no gusubira gukoresha kode.




- **Gutandukanya neza hagati ya Schema na Interface:**


Mu guhingura RGB, Schema (Business Logic) na Interface (ugushikiriza no gukoresha) ni ibigo bibiri vyigenga. Abahinguzi bandika ubuhinga bwa Contract barashobora kwibanda kuri Schema, batababazwa n’ubuhinga bwo gukora canke guserukira amakuru, mu gihe uwundi mugwi (canke uwo mugwi umwe, ariko ku rutonde rw’igihe rutandukanye) ushobora gukora Interface.




- **Uguhinduka guhinduka:**


Interface irashobora guhindurwa canke kwongerwako inyuma y’aho umutungo usohokeye, ataco ukeneye guhindura Contract ubwayo. Ivyo ni itandukaniro rikomeye n'ibindi bikoresho vya On-Chain Smart contract, aho Interface (kenshi ivangwa n'itegeko ry'ugushitsa) ikonjeshwa muri Blockchain.




- Ubushobozi bwa Interface bwinshi


Iryo Contract nyene ryoshobora gushirwa ahabona biciye ku nzira zitandukanye zihuye n’ivyo umuntu akeneye: Interface yoroshe ku muntu akoresha, iyindi iteye imbere cane ku muntu atanga akeneye gucunga ibikorwa vy’imiterere bikomeye. Wallet irashobora rero guhitamwo Interface izozana, bivanye n’ingene ikoreshwa.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/074.webp)


Mu bikorwa, iyo Wallet ironse RGB Contract (biciye muri dosiye `.RGB` canke `.rgba`), irazana kandi Interface ijana, na yo nyene irakoranywa. Mu gihe co gukora, Wallet ishobora, nk'akarorero:




- Suzuma urutonde rw’ibihugu maze usome amazina yavyo, kugira ngo ugaragaze Ticker, Initial Amount, Itariki y’Isohoka, n’ibindi ku mukoresha Interface, aho kugaragaza ikimenyetso c’umubare kitasomwa;
- Kubaka igikorwa (nk'uguhindura) ukoresheje amazina y'ibipimo asobanutse: aho kwandika `ibikorwa { OS_ASSET => 1 }`, bishobora guha umukoresha umwanya "Umubare" mu rupapuro, maze ugahindura aya makuru mu bibanza vyanditswe neza vyitezwe na GW-156.


#### Itandukaniro na Ethereum n'izindi sisitemu


Ku Ethereum, Interface (idondora biciye ku ABI, *Ikoreshwa ry’Ibikoresho Bibiri Interface*) muri rusangi ikomoka kuri kode yabitswe ya On-Chain (Smart contract). Bishobora gutwara amahera menshi canke bikaba bigoye guhindura igice kinaka ca Interface utakoze kuri Contract ubwayo. Ariko rero, RGB ishingiye ku nsiguro yose ya off-chain, n'amakuru ashingiye ku *masezerano* kuri Bitcoin. Iyi nzira ituma bishoboka guhindura Interface (canke ugushirwa mu ngiro kwayo) ataco bihinduye ku mutekano w’ishimikiro wa Contract, kuko kwemeza amategeko y’ubudandaji kuguma muri Schema n’itegeko rya AluVM ryerekanwa.


#### Interface gukoranya


Nk'uko biri kuri Schema, Interface isobanurwa muri kode y'inkomoko (kenshi muri Rust) kandi igakoranywa muri dosiye `.RGB` canke `.rgba`. Iyi dosiye ibiri irimwo amakuru yose asabwa na Wallet kugira ngo:




- Kumenya imirima mu mazina;
- Huza umwanya wose (n’agaciro kawo) n’ubwoko bw’urutonde rukomeye rwasobanuwe muri Contract;
- Menya ibikorwa bitandukanye vyemewe n’ingene wovyubaka.


Igihe Interface imaze kwinjizwa, Wallet irashobora kwerekana neza Contract no gusaba imigenderanire ku wuyikoresha.


### Ibikoresho vyashizweho n'ishirahamwe LNP/BP


Mu bidukikije vya RGB, Interface ikoreshwa mu gutanga insobanuro isomwa kandi ikoreshwa ku makuru n'imikorere ya Contract. Interface rero yuzuza Schema, idondora Business Logic imbere (ubwoko bukomeye, inyandiko zo kwemeza, n’ibindi). Muri iki gice, turaza kuraba interfaces zisanzwe zateguwe n’ishirahamwe LNP/BP ku bwoko rusangi bwa Contract (ibimenyetso bishobora guhinduka, NFT, n’ibindi).


Nk’ukwibutsa, iciyumviro ni uko Interface yose idondora ingene yogaragaza no gukoresha Contract ku ruhande rwa Wallet, ikavuga neza amazina y’ibibanza (nk’i `spec`, `ticker`, `issuedSupply`...) kandi igasobanura ibikorwa bishoboka (nk’i, `T `Guhindura izina`...). Interfaces nyinshi zirasanzwe zikora, ariko hazoba izindi muri kazoza.


#### Ibikoresho bimwe bimwe vyiteguye gukoreshwa


**RGB20** ni Interface ku mitungo ishobora guhinduka, ishobora kugereranywa n’itegeko rya Ethereum ERC20. Ariko rero, iratera intambwe imbere, itanga ibikorwa vyinshi:




- Nk’akarorero, ubushobozi bwo guhindura izina ry’umutungo (guhindura *ticker* canke izina ryose) umaze gusohoka, canke guhindura ukuri kwawo (*stock splits*);
- Ishobora kandi gusobanura uburyo bwo gusubira gusohora ubwa kabiri (bifise aho bigarukira canke bitagira aho bigarukira) no guturira hanyuma bikasubirizwa, kugira ngo bihe uburenganzira uwubitanga bwo gusenya no gusubira kurema ivy’ubutunzi mu gihe hari ibintu bimwebimwe;


Nk’akarorero, RGB20 Interface ishobora guhuzwa n’umugambi wa **Itunga Ridashobora Gufutwa (NIA)**, utegeka Supply y’intango idashobora gufutwa, canke n’iyindi migambi iteye imbere cane nk’uko bisabwa.


**RGB21** yerekeye amasezerano y’ubwoko bwa NFT, canke mu buryo bwagutse, ibirimwo vyose vy’ubuhinga bwa none, nk’uguserukira ibinyamakuru vy’ubuhinga bwa none (amashusho, umuziki, n’ibindi). Uretse gusobanura ikibazo no kwimurira umutungo umwe, harimwo n’ibintu nk’ibi:




- Infashanyo yunze ubumwe yo gushiramwo dosiye (ishika kuri 16 MB) muri Contract (kugira ngo umuntu ayironke ku ruhande rw’umukiriya);
- Ubushobozi bwa nyen'itongo bwo kwinjira "*igicapo*" muri kahise kugira ngo yerekane Ownership ya kera ya NFT.


**RGB25** ni urugero rw'ivy'ubuhinga buhurikiyemwo ibintu bishobora guhinduka n'ibidashobora guhinduka. Igenewe imitungo ishobora guhinduka igice, nk'uguhindura ikimenyetso c'amazu, aho ushaka gucapura umutungo mu gihe uguma ufise uruja n'uruza rw'umutungo w'umuzi umwe (mu yandi majambo, ufise ibice vy'inzu bishobora guhinduka, bihuye n'inzu idashobora guhinduka). Mu buryo bw'ubuhinga, iyo Interface ishobora guhuzwa n'**Itunga Rishobora Gukusanywa (CFA) Schema**, ifata mu muzirikanyi iciyumviro co gucapura mu gihe ikurikirana itunga ry'intango.


#### Ibikoresho biriko birategurwa


Ibindi bikoresho biteguwe gukoreshwa mu buryo bwihariye, ariko ntibiraboneka:




- **RGB22**, yihariye ku bijanye n'ibimenyetso vy'ubuhinga bwa none, kugira ngo icunge ibimenyetso n'imirongo ya On-Chain mu bidukikije vya RGB;
- **RGB23**, ku gutera ikidodo c'igihe giteye imbere, ukoresheje bimwe mu vyiyumviro vya *Opentimestamps*, ariko n'ibiranga gukurikirana;
- **RGB24**, igamije gukorana n'uburyo bw'amazina y'itongo (DNS) busa n'ubwa *Serivisi y'izina rya Ethereum*;
- **RGB26**, igenewe gucunga ama DAO (**Ishirahamwe ryigenga ryegerejwe**) mu buryo bugoranye cane (ubutegetsi, amatora, n'ibindi);
- **RGB30**, isa cane na RGB20 ariko ifise ubudasa bwo kwitwararika ugusohoka kw'intango kwegerejwe no gukoresha Ivyagutse vya Leta. Ivyo vyokoreshwa ku mitungo iyo gusubira gusohoka kwayo icungiwe n'inzego nyinshi, canke ikaba ishingiye ku bintu vyiza kuruta.


Ego ni ko, bivanye n’itariki ubona kuri iri shure, izo nzira zishobora kuba zisanzwe zikora kandi zishobora gukoreshwa.


#### Akarorero ka Interface


Iyi kode ya Rust yerekana [RGB20] (umutungo ushobora guhinduka). Iyi kode yakuwe muri dosiye `rgb20.rs` iri mu bubiko bw'ibitabu bwa RGB. Reka tuvyihweze kugira ngo dutahure imiterere ya Interface n’ingene itanga ikiraro hagati, ku ruhande rumwe, Business Logic (isobanuwe muri Schema) n’ibikorwa vyerekanwa n’amasakoshi n’abakoresha.


```rust
// ...
fn rgb20() -> Iface {
let types = StandardTypes::with(rgb20_stl());

Iface {
version: VerNo::V1,
name: tn!("RGB20"),
global_state: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("spec") => GlobalIface::required(types.get("RGBContract.DivisibleAssetSpec")),
fname!("data") => GlobalIface::required(types.get("RGBContract.ContractData")),
fname!("created") => GlobalIface::required(types.get("RGBContract.Timestamp")),
fname!("issuedSupply") => GlobalIface::one_or_many(types.get("RGBContract.Amount")),
fname!("burnedSupply") => GlobalIface::none_or_many(types.get("RGBContract.Amount")),
fname!("replacedSupply") => GlobalIface::none_or_many(types.get("RGBContract.Amount")),
},
assignments: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("inflationAllowance") => AssignIface::public(OwnedIface::Amount, Req::NoneOrMore),
fname!("updateRight") => AssignIface::public(OwnedIface::Rights, Req::Optional),
fname!("burnEpoch") => AssignIface::public(OwnedIface::Rights, Req::Optional),
fname!("burnRight") => AssignIface::public(OwnedIface::Rights, Req::NoneOrMore),
fname!("assetOwner") => AssignIface::private(OwnedIface::Amount, Req::NoneOrMore),
},
valencies: none!(),
genesis: GenesisIface {
metadata: Some(types.get("RGBContract.IssueMeta")),
global: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("spec") => ArgSpec::required(),
fname!("data") => ArgSpec::required(),
fname!("created") => ArgSpec::required(),
fname!("issuedSupply") => ArgSpec::required(),
},
assignments: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("assetOwner") => ArgSpec::many(),
fname!("inflationAllowance") => ArgSpec::many(),
fname!("updateRight") => ArgSpec::optional(),
fname!("burnEpoch") => ArgSpec::optional(),
},
valencies: none!(),
errors: tiny_bset! {
SUPPLY_MISMATCH,
INVALID_PROOF,
INSUFFICIENT_RESERVES
},
},
transitions: tiny_bmap! {
tn!("Transfer") => TransitionIface {
optional: false,
metadata: None,
globals: none!(),
inputs: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("previous") => ArgSpec::from_non_empty("assetOwner"),
},
assignments: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("beneficiary") => ArgSpec::from_non_empty("assetOwner"),
},
valencies: none!(),
errors: tiny_bset! {
NON_EQUAL_AMOUNTS
},
default_assignment: Some(fname!("beneficiary")),
},
tn!("Issue") => TransitionIface {
optional: true,
metadata: Some(types.get("RGBContract.IssueMeta")),
globals: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("issuedSupply") => ArgSpec::required(),
},
inputs: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("used") => ArgSpec::from_non_empty("inflationAllowance"),
},
assignments: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("beneficiary") => ArgSpec::from_many("assetOwner"),
fname!("future") => ArgSpec::from_many("inflationAllowance"),
},
valencies: none!(),
errors: tiny_bset! {
SUPPLY_MISMATCH,
INVALID_PROOF,
ISSUE_EXCEEDS_ALLOWANCE,
INSUFFICIENT_RESERVES
},
default_assignment: Some(fname!("beneficiary")),
},
tn!("OpenEpoch") => TransitionIface {
optional: true,
metadata: None,
globals: none!(),
inputs: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("used") => ArgSpec::from_required("burnEpoch"),
},
assignments: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("next") => ArgSpec::from_optional("burnEpoch"),
fname!("burnRight") => ArgSpec::required()
},
valencies: none!(),
errors: none!(),
default_assignment: Some(fname!("burnRight")),
},
tn!("Burn") => TransitionIface {
optional: true,
metadata: Some(types.get("RGBContract.BurnMeta")),
globals: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("burnedSupply") => ArgSpec::required(),
},
inputs: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("used") => ArgSpec::from_required("burnRight"),
},
assignments: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("future") => ArgSpec::from_optional("burnRight"),
},
valencies: none!(),
errors: tiny_bset! {
SUPPLY_MISMATCH,
INVALID_PROOF,
INSUFFICIENT_COVERAGE
},
default_assignment: None,
},
tn!("Replace") => TransitionIface {
optional: true,
metadata: Some(types.get("RGBContract.BurnMeta")),
globals: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("replacedSupply") => ArgSpec::required(),
},
inputs: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("used") => ArgSpec::from_required("burnRight"),
},
assignments: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("beneficiary") => ArgSpec::from_many("assetOwner"),
fname!("future") => ArgSpec::from_optional("burnRight"),
},
valencies: none!(),
errors: tiny_bset! {
NON_EQUAL_AMOUNTS,
SUPPLY_MISMATCH,
INVALID_PROOF,
INSUFFICIENT_COVERAGE
},
default_assignment: Some(fname!("beneficiary")),
},
tn!("Rename") => TransitionIface {
optional: true,
metadata: None,
globals: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("new") => ArgSpec::from_required("spec"),
},
inputs: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("used") => ArgSpec::from_required("updateRight"),
},
assignments: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("future") => ArgSpec::from_optional("updateRight"),
},
valencies: none!(),
errors: none!(),
default_assignment: Some(fname!("future")),
},
},
extensions: none!(),
error_type: types.get("RGB20.Error"),
default_operation: Some(tn!("Transfer")),
type_system: types.type_system(),
}
}
```


Muri iyi Interface, turabona ibisa n’imiterere ya Schema: turasanga itangazo rya Global State, Ibihugu vy’Umutungo, Ibikorwa vya Contract (Genesis n’Impinduka), hamwe n’ugutorera umuti amakosa. Ariko Interface yibanda ku kwerekana no gukoresha izo Elements ku Wallet canke ikindi gikorwa ico ari co cose.


Itandukaniro riri hagati ya Schema n’ubwoko bwavyo. Schema ikoresha ubwoko bukomeye (nk'ubwoko `Ubwoko::Unsigned64Bit`) n'ibindi bimenyetso vy'ubuhinga. Interface ikoresha amazina y'ibibanza, ama macro (`izina ry'f!()`, `tn!()`), n'ibisobanuro vy'imigwi y'imvo (`ArgSpec`, `Igishushanyo::Uburenganzira`...). Intumbero aha ni ugufasha gutahura no gutunganya ibikorwa vya Elements ku Wallet.


Ikindi, Interface ishobora gushiramwo ibindi bikorwa ku Schema y'ishimikiro (nk'ugucungera uburenganzira bwa `burnEpoch`), igihe cose ivyo biguma bihuye n'ubwenge bwa nyuma bwemejwe ku ruhande rw'umukiriya. Igice ca AluVM "inyandiko" muri Schema kizotuma habaho ukuri kw'inyandiko, mu gihe Interface idondora ingene umukoresha (canke Wallet) akorana n'izo ntara n'ihinduka.


#### Global State n’Ibikorwa


Mu gice ca `global_state`, dusanga ivyicaro nka `spec` (insobanuro y'umutungo), `amakuru`, `yaremwe`, `Itanga`, `Itanga yaturiwe`, `Itanga yasubirijwe`. Ivyo ni ibibanza Wallet ishobora gusoma no gushikiriza. Nk'akarorero:




- `spec` izokwerekana imiterere ya token;
- `issuedSupply` canke `burnedSupply` biduha umubare wose w'ibimenyetso vyasohowe canke vyaturiwe, n'ibindi.


Mu gice ca `ibikorwa`, turasobanura uruhara canke uburenganzira butandukanye. Nk'akarorero:




- `assetOwner` ihuye n'ugufata ibimenyetso (ni *Owned State* ishobora guhinduka);
- `burnRight` ihuye n'ubushobozi bwo guturira ibimenyetso;
- updateRight` ihuye n'uburenganzira bwo guhindura izina ry'umutungo.


Ijambo ry'ingenzi `ry'abantu bose' canke 'ry'ibanga` (nk'akarorero `AssignIface::iry'abantu bose(...)`) ryerekana nimba izo ntara ziboneka (`abantu bose`) canke ibanga (`ibanga`). Naho `Req::NtaCankeIbindi`, `Req::Ihitamwo`, vyerekana ivyitezwe.


#### Genesis n'imihindukire


Igice ca `Genesis` kidondora ingene umutungo utangura:




- Ivyo `ibisobanuro`, `amakuru`, `vyaremwe`, `vyasohowe` ni ngombwa (`ArgSpec::bisabwa()`);
- Ibikorwa nka `assetOwner` bishobora kuba biri mu makopi menshi (`ArgSpec::many()`), bikaba vyemerera ibimenyetso gukwiragizwa ku bafise benshi b'intango;
- Ivyimburwa nka `Igihe c'Iterambere` canke `Igihe c'Igihe` bishobora (canke ntibishobora) gushirwa muri Genesis.


Hanyuma, ku Nzira yose (`Kwimurira`, `Ikibazo`, `Guturira`...), Interface isobanura ivyicaro igikorwa citeze nk'inyungu, ivyicaro igikorwa kizotanga nk'isohoka, n'amakosa yose yoshobora kubaho. Nk'akarorero:


**Guhinduka:**




- Ivyinjijwe: `imbere` → bitegerezwa kuba `Umutungo`;
- Inshingano: `uwuronka inyungu` → azoba `Nyitunga` mushasha;
- Ikosa: `NON_EQUAL_AMOUNTS` (Wallet izoshobora rero gukorana n'ibibazo aho umubare w'injiza udahuye n'umubare w'isohoka).


**Ikibazo `Impinduka`:**




- Ihitamwo (`ihitamwo: ukuri`), nk'uko ivyimburwa vy'inyongera bitakoreshwa vy'ukuri;
- Ivyinjijwe: `vyakoreshejwe` → `InflationAllowance`, ni ukuvuga uruhusha rwo kwongerako ibindi bimenyetso;
- Inshingano: `uwuronka inyungu` (ibimenyetso bishasha vyaronswe) na `akazoza` (ibisigaye `InflationAllowance`);
- Amakosa ashoboka: `GUTANGA_NTIBIHUYE`, `IKIBAZO_KIRENZE_IBIMENYETSO`, n'ibindi.


**Ihinduka ry'uguturira:**




- Ivyinjijwe: `vyakoreshejwe` → a `guturiraIburyo`;
- Globals: `Ivyo Gutanga` vyaturitse` birakenewe;
- Inshingano: `akazoza` → ugukomeza gushoboka kwa `burnRight` nimba tutaturiye vyose;
- Amakosa: `GUTANGA_BITAHURA`, `IKIMENYETSO_KIDAKORA`, `IBIMENYETSO_BITAHAGIJE`.


Igikorwa kimwekimwe cose rero kiradondaguwe mu buryo bushobora gusomwa kuri Wallet. Ivyo bituma bishoboka kugaragaza igishushanyo Interface aho umukoresha ashobora kubona neza: "Ufise uburenganzira bwo guturira. Woba wipfuza guturira umubare kanaka? Kode irazi kwuzuza umwanya wa `burnedSupply` maze ikagenzura ko `burnRight` ari ukuri."


Mu ncamake, birahambaye kwibuka ko Interface, naho yoba yuzuye gute, ubwayo itasobanura ivyiyumviro vy'imbere vya Contract. Umutima w’igikorwa ukorwa na **Schema**, irimwo ubwoko bukomeye, imiterere ya Genesis, inzira z’uguhinduka n’ibindi. Interface gusa igaragaza izo Elements mu buryo busanzwe kandi bufise izina, kugira ngo zikoreshwe mu gikorwa.


Kubera ubuhinga bwa RGB, Interface irashobora gusubirwamwo (nk'akarorero, mu kwongerako `Guhindura izina`, gukosora iyerekanwa ry'umurima, n'ibindi) ataco ukeneye kwandika Contract yose. Abakoresha iyi Interface barashobora rero kwungukira kuri ivyo bintu vyiza, bakimara guhindura dosiye `.RGB` canke `.rgba`.


Ariko umaze gutangaza Interface, ukeneye kuyihuza na Schema ihuye. Ibi bikorwa biciye kuri ***Interface Implementation***, igaragaza ingene woshiramwo ikarita y'umwanya wose ufise izina (nk'izina ry'f!("Nyitungo")`) ku ID ikomeye (nk'iyi `OS_ASSET`) isobanuwe muri Schema. Ivyo bituma, nk'akarorero, iyo Wallet ikoresheje umurima wa `burnRight`, iyo ni yo nzira, muri Schema, idondora ubushobozi bwo guturira ibimenyetso.


### Interface Implementation


Mu nyubakwa ya RGB, twabonye ko igice cose (Schema, Interface, n’ibindi) gishobora gutegurwa no gukoranirizwa ku giti caco. Ariko rero, haracariho ikintu kimwe gihambaye gihuza ivyo bice vy'inyubako bitandukanye: ***Interface Implementation***. Ivyo ni vyo bigaragaza neza ibimenyetso canke ivyicaro vyasobanuwe muri Schema (ku ruhande rwa Business Logic) ku mazina yamenyeshejwe muri Interface (ku ruhande rw’ugushikiriza n’ugukorana n’abakoresha). Rero iyo Wallet ishize Contract, irashobora gutahura neza neza ikibanza gihuye n'iki, n'ingene igikorwa citwa muri Interface gifitaniye isano n'ubwenge bwa Schema.


Iciyumviro gihambaye ni uko Interface Implementation atari ngombwa ko igaragaza ibikorwa vyose vya Schema, canke ivyicaro vyose vya Interface: ishobora kugarukira ku gice gitoyi. Mu bikorwa, ivyo bituma bishoboka kubuza canke gucungera imice imwimwe ya Schema. Nk'akarorero, woshobora kugira Schema ifise ubwoko bune bw'ibikorwa, ariko Implementation Interface igaragaza bibiri gusa muri vyo mu gihe kinaka. Ku rundi ruhande, iyo Interface itanga izindi ntumbero z’iherezo, turashobora guhitamwo kutazishira mu ngiro hano.


Aha ni akarorero ka kera ka Interface Implementation, aho dufatanya *Itunga Ridashobora Gufutwa* (NIA) Schema na RGB20 Interface:


```rust
fn nia_rgb20() -> IfaceImpl {
let schema = nia_schema();
let iface = Rgb20::iface();

IfaceImpl {
version: VerNo::V1,
schema_id: schema.schema_id(),
iface_id: iface.iface_id(),
script: none!(),
global_state: tiny_bset! {
NamedField::with(GS_NOMINAL, fname!("spec")),
NamedField::with(GS_DATA, fname!("data")),
NamedField::with(GS_TIMESTAMP, fname!("created")),
NamedField::with(GS_ISSUED_SUPPLY, fname!("issuedSupply")),
},
assignments: tiny_bset! {
NamedField::with(OS_ASSET, fname!("assetOwner")),
},
valencies: none!(),
transitions: tiny_bset! {
NamedType::with(TS_TRANSFER, tn!("Transfer")),
},
extensions: none!(),
}
}
```


Muri iyi Nshirwa mu ngiro Interface:




- Turavuga neza Schema, biciye ku `nia_schema()`, na Interface, biciye ku `Rgb20::iface()`. Ivyo bimenyetso bikoreshwa kugira ngo Anchor Interface Implementation ku ruhande rwo gukoranya (ivyo bifatanya ibimenyetso vy'ibanga vy'ivyo bice bibiri);
- Ikarata ishirwaho hagati ya Schema Elements na Interface Elements. Nk'akarorero, `GS_NOMINAL` umwanya muri Schema uhuye n'urudodo `"spec"` ku ruhande rwa Interface (`UmwanyaWizina::na(GS_IZINA, fizina!("spec"))`). Turakora ukwo nyene ku bikorwa, nka `TS_TRANSFER`, ivyo duhuza na `"Kwimurira"` muri Interface...;
- Turashobora kubona ko ata n’imwe ifise ubushobozi (`ubushobozi: nta n’umwe!()`) canke ivyungura (`ivyungura: nta n’imwe!()`), bikaba vyerekana ko iyi NIA Contract idakoresha ivyo bimenyetso.


Igisubizo inyuma yo gukoranya ni dosiye itandukanye `.RGB` canke `.rgba`, izokwinjizwa muri Wallet yongerako Schema na Interface. Gutyo, iyo porogarama irazi ingene yohuza neza iyi NIA Contract (iyo ivyiyumviro vyayo bidondora na Schema yayo) na "RGB20" Interface (itanga amazina y'abantu n'uburyo bwo gukorana n'ibimenyetso bishobora guhinduka), ikoresha iyi GW-166 nk'inzira ibiri hagati y'ivyo bibiri.


#### Ni kuki twotandukanya Interface Implementation?


Gutandukana biratuma umuntu ashobora guhindura uko abona ibintu. Schema imwe yoshobora kugira Ibikorwa vyinshi bitandukanye vya Interface, kimwe cose kikaba kigaragaza ibikorwa bitandukanye. Ikindi, Interface Implementation ubwayo irashobora guhinduka canke gusubira kwandikwa ataco bisaba guhindura haba muri Schema canke Interface. Ivyo bigumya ingingo ngenderwako ya RGB y’uguhinduranya: igice cose (Schema, Interface, Interface Implementation) gishobora guhindurwa no guhindurwa kidasanzwe, igihe cose amategeko y’uguhuza yashizweho n’amasezerano yubahirijwe (ibimenyetso bimwe, uguhuza ubwoko, n’ibindi).


Mu gukoresha beton, iyo Wallet itwara Contract, itegerezwa:




- Ishiremwo **Schema** yashizwe hamwe (kugira ngo umenye imiterere ya Business Logic);
- Ugushiramwo **Interface** (kugira ngo utahure amazina n'ibikorwa vyo ku ruhande rw'ukoresha);
- Umuzigo washizwe hamwe **Interface Implementation** (kugira ngo uhuze ubuhinga bwa Schema n'amazina ya Interface, igikorwa ku gikorwa, umurima ku murima).


Ubu buhinga bwo kwubaka buratuma bishoboka gukoresha ibintu nk'ibi:




- Guhagarika ibikorwa bimwebimwe ku bakoresha bamwebamwe: gutanga igice c’Ishirwa mu ngiro Interface gitanga gusa uburenganzira bwo gukoresha amafaranga y’ishimikiro, ata gutanga ibikorwa vyo guturira canke guhindura, nk’akarorero;
- Guhindura ukuntu ivyerekanywe: guhingura Interface Implementation ihindura izina ry’umurima uri muri Interface canke ukayishushanya mu buryo butandukanye, ata guhindura ishingiro rya Contract;
- Gushigikira imigambi myinshi: Wallet ishobora gushiramwo Ibikorwa vyinshi vya Interface ku bwoko bumwe bwa Interface, kugira ngo ikoreshe imigambi itandukanye (imirongo itandukanye ya token), igihe cose imiterere yayo ihuye.


Mu gice gikurikira, turaza kuraba ingene uguhererekanya amafaranga Contract gukora, n’ingene amafagitire ya RGB akora.


## Contract kwimurira


<chapterId>f043a307-d420-5752-b0d7-ebfd845802c0</chapterId>


:::id ya videwo=75eb5a8d-1910-4155-b5e3-81204c9a8901:::


Muri iki gice, turaza gusuzuma ingene Contract igenda mu bidukikije vya RGB. Kugira ngo ivyo tubigereranye, turaza kuraba Alice na Bob, abakinnyi bacu basanzwe, bipfuza ko Exchange iba umutungo wa RGB. Tuzokwereka kandi ibice bimwe bimwe vy'amabwirizwa bivuye mu gikoresho c'umurongo w'amabwirizwa `RGB`, kugira ngo turabe ingene bikora mu bikorwa.


### Gutahura RGB Contract kwimurira


Reka dufate akarorero k'uguhindura hagati ya Alice na Bob. Muri aka karorero, twiyumvira ko Bob ariko aratangura gukoresha RGB, mu gihe Alice asanzwe afise itunga rya RGB muri Wallet yiwe. Turabona ingene Bob ashiraho ibidukikije vyiwe, akazana Contract bibereye, hanyuma agasaba kwimurirwa kuri Alice, n'ingene Alice akora igikorwa nyaco kuri Bitcoin Blockchain.


#### 1) Gushiramwo RGB Wallet


Mbere na mbere, Bob ikeneye gushiramwo RGB Wallet, ni ukuvuga porogarama ihuye n’itegeko. Ivyo nta masezerano arimwo mu ntango. Bob na yo nyene izokenera:




- Igikoresho ca Bitcoin Wallet co gucunga ama UTXO yawe;
- Ihuzwa n’urudodo rwa Bitcoin (canke n’umurongo wa Electrum), kugira ngo ushobore kumenya UTXO zawe no gukwiragiza amafaranga yawe ku rubuga.


Nk’ukwibutsa, **Ibihugu vy’Igihugu** muri RGB vyerekeye UTXO za Bitcoin. Tubwirizwa rero kwama dushobora gucunga no gukoresha UTXOs mu bikorwa vya Bitcoin birimwo amasezerano y’ubuhinga bwa none (`Tapret` canke `Opret`) yerekana amakuru ya RGB.


#### 2) Contract kuronka amakuru


Bob rero arakeneye kugarura amakuru ya Contract akunda. Aya makuru ashobora gukwiragira biciye ku nzira iyo ari yo yose: urubuga, e-mail, ubutumwa... Mu bikorwa, ashirwa hamwe muri ***Consignment***, ni ukuvuga agapaki gatoyi k'amakuru karimwo:




- **Genesis**, isobanura uko Contract yari imeze mu ntango;
- **Schema**, idondora Business Logic (ubwoko bukomeye, inyandiko zo kwemeza, n’ibindi);
- **Interface**, isobanura ikiganiro Layer (amazina y'ibibanza, ibikorwa bishobora gushikwako);
- **Interface Implementation**, ihuza neza Schema na Interface.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/075.webp)


Ingano yose hamwe akenshi iba ingana n’amakilobyte makeyi, kuko igice kimwekimwe cose muri rusangi gipima amabayite makeyi. Bishobora kandi gushoboka gutangaza iyi Consignment muri Base58, biciye ku nzira zidashobora gucengera (nka Nostr canke biciye ku Lightning Network, nk’akarorero), canke nk’akarorero ka QR code.


#### 3) Contract kwinjiza no kwemeza


Igihe Bob amaze kwakira Consignment, arayishira mu RGB Wallet yiwe. Ivyo bizoheza:




- Suzuma ko Genesis na Schema zifise akamaro;
- Umuzigo Interface na Interface Implementation;
- Kuvugurura amakuru y'umukiriya wawe Stash.


Bob ubu arashobora kubona umutungo uri muri Wallet yiwe (naho yoba atarawugira) agatahura amatongo ariho, ibikorwa bishoboka... Aca akenera guhamagara umuntu afise vy’ukuri uwo mutungo azokwimurirwa. Mu karorero kacu, iyi ni Alice.


Inzira yo kumenya uwufise umutungo kanaka wa RGB isa n’ukurondera uwuyitanga Bitcoin. Ivyerekeye iyo nzira y’uguhuza bivana n’ikoreshwa (amasoko, imihora y’ubutumwa bwigenga, gutanga invoice, ugurisha ibintu n’ibikorwa, umushahara...).


#### 4) Gutanga urupapuro rwa Invoice


Kugira ngo utangure kwimurira umutungo wa RGB, Bob itegerezwa kubanza gutanga Invoice. Iyi Invoice ikoreshwa mu:




- Bwira Alice ubwoko bw'igikorwa kizokorwa (nk'akarorero, `Ukwimurira` kuva kuri RGB20 Interface);
- Gutanga Alice *Seal Definition* ya Bob (ni ukuvuga UTXO aho yipfuza kwakira umutungo);
- Sobanura umubare w’ibirungo bikora bisabwa (nk’akarorero, ibice 100).


Bob ikoresha igikoresho `RGB` ku murongo w'amabwirizwa. Twibaze ko ashaka ibice 100 vya token `ContractId` yayo izwi, ashaka kwizigira `Tapret`, kandi agasobanura UTXO yayo (`456e3..dfe1:0`):


```bash
bob$ rgb invoice RGB20 100 <ContractId> tapret1st:456e3..dfe1:0
```


Turaza kuraba neza imiterere y’amafagitire ya RGB mu mpera y’iki kigabane.


#### 5) Ugutanga Invoice


Invoice yashizweho (nk'akarorero nk'URL: `RGB:2WBcas9.../RGB20/100+utxob:...`) irimwo amakuru yose Alice ikeneye kugira ngo itegure ukwimurira. Nk'uko biri kuri Consignment, ishobora gushirwa mu buryo bubereye (Base58 canke ubundi buryo) maze ikarungikwa biciye ku butumwa, e-mail, Nostr...


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/076.webp)


#### 6) Gutegura ibikorwa ku ruhande rwa Alice


Alice yakira Invoice ya Bob. Mu gitabu ciwe ca RGB Wallet, afise igitabu ca Stash kirimwo umutungo azokwimurirwa. Kugira ngo akoreshe UTXO irimwo umutungo, ategerezwa kubanza gutanga PSBT (*Partially Signed Bitcoin Transaction*), ni ukuvuga Bitcoin idatunganye, akoresheje UTXO afise:


```bash
alice$ wallet construct tx.psbt
```


Iyi nzira y'ishimikiro (itashizweko umukono muri iki gihe) izokoreshwa kuri Anchor Commitment y'ibanga ihuye n'uguhindura kuri Bob. Alice izokoreshwa, kandi mu gisohoka, tuzoshiramwo `Tapret` canke `Opret` Commitment ku Bob.


#### 7) Uruvyaro rw'uguhindura Consignment


Inyuma y'aho, Alice yubaka ***Terminal Consignment*** (rimwe na rimwe yitwa "kwimurira Consignment") biciye ku itegeko:


```bash
alice$ rgb transfer tx.psbt <invoice> consignment.rgb
```


Iyi dosiye nshasha irimwo:




- Amateka yose y’Impinduka za Leta zasabwa kugira ngo umutungo wemezwe gushika n’ubu (kuva Genesis);
- Itegeko rishasha rya State Transition ryimura ivy’ubutunzi kuva kuri Alice rikaja muri Bob, hakurikijwe Invoice Bob ryasohoye;
- Igikorwa kidatunganye ca Bitcoin (*Witness Transaction*) (`tx.PSBT`), gikoresha Alice ca Alice, cahinduwe kugira ngo kigiremwo Commitment ku Bob.


Muri iki gihe, iyo nzira y’ugucuruza ntiyigeze itangazwa ku rubuga rwa Bitcoin. Consignment ni nini kuruta Consignment y’ishimikiro, kuko irimwo amateka yose (*uruzitiro rw’ibimenyamenya*) kugira ngo yerekane ko umutungo ubereye.


#### 8) Bob irasuzuma kandi yemera Consignment


Alice irungika iyi **Terminal Consignment** kuri Bob. Bob izoca:




- Gusuzuma ko igitabu ca State Transition gifise ukuri (kumenya ko amateka ahuye, ko amategeko ya Contract yubahirizwa, n’ibindi);
- Wongereko Stash yo mu karere iwanyu;
- Birashoboka ko generate umukono (`sig:...`) kuri Consignment, kugira ngo yerekane ko yasuzumwe kandi yemejwe (rimwe na rimwe yitwa "*igitabu c'umushahara*").


```bash
bob$ rgb accept consignment.rgb
sig:DbwzvSu4BZU81jEpE9FVZ3xjcyuTKWWy2gmdnaxtACrS
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/077.webp)


#### 9) Uburyo: Bob yohereza ivyemezo kuri Alice (*igitabu c'amahera*)


Niba Bob abishaka, arashobora gusubiza iyo sinya kuri Alice. Ivyo vyerekana:




- Ko yemera ko iyo mpinduka ari ngirakamaro;
- Ko yemera ko igikorwa ca Bitcoin gitangazwa.


Ivyo si ngombwa, ariko birashobora gutuma Alice yizigira ko ata ntambara zizokurikira ku bijanye n’ukwimurirwa.


#### 10) Alice ishira umukono kandi itangaza ivy’ugucuruza


Alice ishobora rero:




- Suzuma umukono wa Bob (`RGB suzuma <sig>`);
- Sinya kuri *Witness Transaction* ikiri ikimenyetso ca PSBT (`Ikimenyetso ca Wallet`);
- Gusohora Witness Transaction ku rubuga rwa Bitcoin (`-sohora`).


```bash
alice$ rgb check <sig>
alice$ wallet sign —publish tx.psbt
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/078.webp)


Iyo yemejwe, iyo nzira y’ugucuruza ikimenyetso c’iherezo ry’ugutanga. Bob aba ari we nyen’umutungo mushasha: ubu afise Owned State yerekana UTXO agenzura, ivyo bikaba vyemezwa n’ukubaho kwa Commitment mu gucuruza.


Mu ncamake, ng’iyi inzira yose yo kwimurira:


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/079.webp)


### Inyungu z'uguhindura RGB




- **Ibanga**:


Alice na Bob ni zo zonyene zishobora kuronka amakuru yose ya State Transition. Ba Exchange aya makuru hanze ya Blockchain, biciye ku vyoherezwa. Ivyemezo vy’ubuhinga bwa none mu gucuruza Bitcoin ntivyerekana ubwoko bw’itunga canke umubare, ivyo bikaba bitanga ibanga rikomeye cane kuruta ibindi bikoresho vya On-Chain token.




- **Kwemeza uruhande rw'umukiriya**:


Bob ishobora kugenzura ukuntu ivyo kwimurirwa bihuye mu kugereranya **Consignment** n'ibifatanya biri muri Bitcoin Blockchain. Ntakeneye kwemezwa n'uwundi muntu. Alice ntibwirizwa gutangaza amateka yose kuri Blockchain, ivyo bigabanya umuzigo ku bijanye n'umurongo w'ishimikiro kandi bikaba bituma haba ibanga.




- **Ubutome bworoshe**:


Ivyiyumviro bikomeye (ivy’uguhinduranya atome hagati ya BTC n’umutungo wa RGB, nk’akarorero) birashobora gukorwa mu gihe c’uguhinduranya rimwe, bikaba bikirinda gukenera inyandiko za HTLC canke PTLC. Iyo amasezerano atamenyeshejwe, umuntu wese arashobora gusubira gukoresha ama UTXO yiwe mu bundi buryo.


### Igishushanyo c'incamake c'ukwimurira


Imbere yo kuraba amafagitire mu buryo burambuye, ng’iki igishushanyo c’incamake c’urugendo rwose rw’uguhererekanya amafaranga RGB:




- Bob ishiraho RGB Wallet maze ironka Contract Consignment ya mbere;
- Bob itanga Invoice ivuga UTXO aho umuntu yokwakira umutungo;
- Alice yakira Invoice, yubaka PSBT maze ivyara Terminal Consignment;
- Bob aravyemera, akavyisuzuma, akongerako amakuru kuri Stash yiwe, agashirako umukono (*payslip*) iyo bikenewe;
- Alice itangaza ivy’ugucuruza ku rubuga rwa Bitcoin;
- Kwemeza ivy’ugucuruza bituma ivyo kwimurira biba ivy’ubutegetsi.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/080.webp)


Iryo shirahamwe ryerekana ububasha bwose n’uguhinduranya kw’amasezerano ya RGB: Exchange yigenga, yemejwe ku ruhande rw’umukiriya, ishizweho mu buryo buke kandi buteye ubwoba kuri Bitcoin Blockchain, kandi igumya umutekano mwiza w’amasezerano (nta ngorane ya Double-spending). Ivyo bituma RGB iba ikibanza ciza co gutanga agaciro k’ibintu bifise ibanga kandi bishobora guhindurwa kuruta On-Chain blockchains zishobora gukoreshwa.


### Inyemezabuguzi RGB


Muri iki gice, turasigura mu buryo burambuye ingene **amafagitire** akora mu bidukikije vya RGB n'ingene ashoboza ibikorwa (cane cane ukwimurira) bikorwa na Contract. Ubwa mbere, turaza kuraba ibimenyetso bikoreshwa, hanyuma turabe ingene bishirwa mu nzira, hanyuma turabe imiterere ya Invoice igaragazwa nk’URL (uburyo bubereye gukoreshwa mu bikoresho).


#### Ibiranga n'ugushiramwo


Ikimenyetso kidasanzwe kirasobanurwa kuri buri kimwe muri ibi bikurikira Elements:




- Igitabu c’umwaka w’1883;
- Igitabu caco c’umwaka w’1885 (Igitabu c’umwaka w’1884);
- Igitabu caco c’umwaka w’1887 n’ica 1886;
- Itunga ryayo (ibimenyetso, NFT, n’ibindi),


Ukwo kudasanzwe ni ikintu gihambaye cane, kuko igice cose c’urwo rutonde kigomba kuba gishobora gutandukanywa. Nk’akarorero, Contract X ntitegerezwa gutera urujijo n’iyindi Contract Y, kandi interfaces zibiri zitandukanye (RGB20 vs. RGB21, nk’akarorero) zitegerezwa kuba zifise ibimenyetso bitandukanye.


Kugira ngo ivyo bimenyetso bibe vyiza (bito) kandi bishobore gusomwa, dukoresha:




- Base58 encoding, irinda gukoresha inyuguti zitera urujijo (nk'akarorero `0` n'urudome `O`) kandi itanga imirongo miremire;
- Intangamarara yerekana kamere y’ikimenyetso, akenshi mu buryo bwa `RGB:` canke URN isa n’iyo.


Nk'akarorero, `ContractId` yoshobora guserukirwa n'ikintu nk'iki:


```txt
rgb:2WBcas9-yjzEvGufY-9GEgnyMj7-beMNMWA8r-sPHtV1nPU-TMsGMQX
```


Imbere ya `RGB:` yemeza ko iki ari ikimenyetso ca RGB, kandi atari ihuriro rya HTTP canke uwundi murongo. Kubera iyo ntango, amasakoshi arashobora gusobanura neza urudodo.


#### Ugucapura kw'indanga


Ivyerekana RGB akenshi birareha cane, kuko umutekano wo munsi (cryptographic) ushobora gusaba ivyicaro vy’ibice 256 canke birenze. Kugira ngo umuntu ashobore gusoma no kugenzura, *duca* iyo mirongo mu bice vyinshi bitandukanijwe n'akarongo (`-`). Rero, aho kugira uruzitiro rurerure rw’ibimenyetso rudacitse, turarugabanyamwo ibice bigufi. Ico gikorwa kirasanzwe ku bijanye n’ikarata y’inguzanyo canke inomero za telefone, kandi kirakora no ngaha kugira ngo umuntu ashobore kugenzura neza. Rero, nk'akarorero, umukoresha canke umufatanyabikorwa arashobora kubwirwa ati: "*Ndagusavye usuzume ko igice ca gatatu ari `9GEgnyMj7`*", aho kugereranya vyose icarimwe. Igipande ca nyuma gikoreshwa kenshi nk'**checksum**, kugira ngo hagire uburyo bwo kumenya amakosa canke amakosa yo kwandika.


Nk'akarorero, `ContractId` muri base58 ishobora kuba:


```txt
2WBcas9-yjzEvGufY-9GEgnyMj7-beMNMWA8r-sPHtV1nPU-TMsGMQX
```


Imwe muri izo nzira imenagura urudodo mu bice. Ivyo ntibigira ico bikoze ku nsobanuro y’itegeko, ahubwo bigira ico bikoze ku kuntu rigaragazwa gusa.


#### Gukoresha URLs ku mafagitire


Igitabo ca RGB Invoice kigaragazwa nk'URL. Ivyo bisigura ko umuntu ashobora kuyikanda canke kuyicapura (nk’uko ari kode ya QR), kandi Wallet ishobora kuyisobanura ata guca ku ruhande kugira ngo umuntu akore igikorwa. Ukwo gukorana kworoshe gutandukanye n’izindi nzira zimwe zimwe aho utegerezwa gukopa no gushiramwo amakuru atandukanye mu bice bitandukanye vyo muri porogarama.


Invoice ku token ishobora guhinduka (nk'akarorero RGB20 token) ishobora gusa n'iyi:


```txt
rgb:2WBcas9-yjzEvGufY-9GEgnyMj7-beMNMWA8r-sPHtV1nPU-TMsGMQX/RGB20/100+utxob:egXsFnw-5Eud7WKYn-7DVQvcPbc-rR69YmgmG-veacwmUFo-uMFKFb
```


Reka dusuzume iyi URL:




- `RGB:`** (intango): yerekana ihuriro rikoresha umurongo wa RGB (bisa n'ivyo `http:` canke `Bitcoin:` mu bindi bihe);
- **igereranya**: igereranya `ContractId` ya token ushaka gukoresha;
- `/RGB20/100`: yerekana ko `RGB20` Interface ikoreshwa kandi ko ibice 100 vy'umutungo bisabwa. Inyuguti ni: `/Interface/umubare`;
- `+utxob:`**: isobanura ko amakuru yerekeye uwuronka UTXO (canke, mu buryo bubereye, insobanuro ya Single-Use Seal) yongeweko;
- **Seal**: iyi ni *blinded* UTXO (canke Seal Definition). Mu yandi majambo, Bob yarapfutse UTXO yiwe nyayo, rero uwuyirungitse (Alice) ntazi ico Address nyayo ari co. Azi gusa ko hariho Seal ikora yerekeza kuri UTXO igenzurwa na Bob.


Kuba vyose bifatanya na URL imwe bituma ubuzima bworoha ku muntu abikoresha: gukanda canke gucapura mu Wallet, igikorwa kikaba giteguwe gukorwa.


Umuntu yoshobora kwiyumvira uburyo aho igiharuro coroshe (nk'akarorero `USDT`) gikoreshwa aho gukoresha `ContractId`. Ariko ivyo vyotuma haba ingorane zikomeye z’ukwizigirana n’umutekano: igiharuro si ikintu kidasanzwe (amasezerano menshi yoshobora kuvuga ko yitwa `USDT`). Na RGB, turashaka ikimenyetso kidasanzwe, kitagiramwo amakenga. Ni co gituma kwemera urudodo rw’ibice 256, rwashizwe muri base58 kandi rwaciwemwo ibice. Uwukoresha arazi ko ariko arakoresha neza na neza Contract ID yayo ari `2WBcas9-yjz...` atari uwundi.


#### Ibindi bipimo vya URL


Ushobora kandi kwongerako ibindi bipimo kuri URL, mu buryo bumwe na HTTP, nka:


```txt
rgb:2WBcas9-yjzEvGufY-9GEgnyMj7-beMNMWA8r-sPHtV1nPU-TMsGMQX/RGB20/100+utxob:egXsFnw-5Eud7WKYn-7DVQvcPbc-rR69YmgmG-veacwmUFo-uMFKFb?sig=6kzbKKffP6xftkxn9UP8gWqiC41W16wYKE5CYaVhmEve
```




- `?sig=...`: igereranya, nk'akarorero, umukono ufitaniye isano na Invoice, uwo amasakoshi amwe amwe ashobora kugenzura;
- Iyo Wallet idacungera iyo sinyatire, yirengagiza gusa iyo parametere.


Reka dufate urugero rwa NFT biciye kuri RGB21 Interface. Nk’akarorero, twoshobora kugira:


```txt
rgb:7BKsac8-beMNMWA8r-3GEprtFh7-bjzEvGufY-aNLuU4nSN-MRsLOIK/RGB21/DbwzvSu-4BZU81jEp-E9FVZ3xj-cyuTKWWy-2gmdnaxt-ACrS+utxob:egXsFnw-5Eud7WKYn-7DVQvcPbc-rR69YmgmG-veacwmUFo-uMFKFb
```


Aha turabona:




- `RGB:`**: Intangiriro ya URL;
- 1917 ID (NFT);
- **rGB21**: Interface ku mitungo idashobora guhinduka (NFT);
- **`DbwzvSu-4BZU81jEp-...`**: ivyerekeye igice kidasanzwe ca NFT, nk'akarorero Hash y'amakuru (ivy'amakuru, amakuru y'imbere...);
- `+utxob: nk'akarorero: 1920.


Iciyumviro ni kimwe: gutanga uruja n’uruza rudasanzwe Wallet ishobora gusobanura, rugaragaza neza umutungo udasanzwe uzorungikwa.


#### Ibindi bikorwa biciye kuri URL


RGB URLs ntizikoreshwa gusa mu gusaba kwimurira. Bashobora kandi gushiramwo ibikorwa biteye imbere cane, nk’ugutanga ibimenyetso bishasha (*issuance*). Nk'akarorero:


```txt
rgb:2WBcas9-yjzEvGufY-9GEgnyMj7-beMNMWA8r-sPHtV1nPU-TMsGMQX/RGB20/issue/100000+utxob:egXsFnw-5Eud7WKYn-7DVQvcPbc-rR69YmgmG-veacwmUFo-uMFKFb
```


Aha niho dusanga:




- `RGB:`: amategeko;
- `2Ibibazo9-...`: Indangamuntu ya Contract;
- `/RGB20/ikibazo/100000`: yerekana ko ushaka guhamagara "*Ikibazo*" kugira ngo ureme ibindi bimenyetso 100.000;
- `+Igisubizo:`: Seal Definition.


Nk'akarorero, Wallet yoshobora gusoma ngo: "Nasabwe gukora igikorwa co gukuraho ikibazo kuva kuri `RGB20` Interface, kuri Contract nk'iyo, ku bice 100.000, ku nyungu ya Contract nk'iyo".


None ko twabonye Elements nyamukuru ya porogarama ya RGB, nzobajana mu kigabane gikurikira ku buryo bwo gukora RGB Contract.


## Gutegura amasezerano y'ubwenge


<chapterId>0e0a645c-0049-588d-8965-b8c536590cc9</chapterId>


:::id ya videwo=a3ad6dcd-90b8-4272-9dfc-76c85c859167::


Muri iki gice, tuzofata intambwe ku yindi uburyo bwo kwandika Contract, dukoresheje igikoresho c'umurongo w'amabwirizwa `RGB`. Intumbero ni ukwerekana ingene woshiramwo no gukoresha CLI, ugakoranya **Schema**, ​​ugashiramwo **Interface** na **Interface Implementation**, hanyuma ugatanga (*ugutanga*) umutungo. Turaza kuraba kandi ivyiyumviro bishingiyeko, harimwo n’ugukoranya n’ugushingira intahe. Mu mpera z’iki gice, ukwiye kuba ushoboye gusubiramwo iyo nzira no kwihingurira amasezerano yawe bwite ya RGB.


Nk’ukwibutsa, ubuhinga bwo mu mutima bwa RGB bushingiye ku masomero ya Rust mwebwe nk’abahinguzi, mushobora kwinjiza mu migambi yanyu kugira ngo mucunge igice ca Client-side Validation. Ikindi, umugwi w’ishirahamwe LNP/BP uriko urakora ibijanye n’ugufatanya ibitabu vy’izindi ndimi, ariko ivyo ntibiraheza. Ikindi, izindi nzego nka Bitfinex ziriko zirategura ibirundo vyazo vy’ubufatanye (ivyo tuzobivuga mu bice 2 vya nyuma vy’amashure). Kugeza rero, `RGB` CLI ni co gikoreshwa mu buryo butegekanijwe, naho coba kiguma kidasukuye cane.


### Gushiramwo no gushikiriza igikoresho ca RGB


Itegeko nyamukuru ryitwa gusa `RGB`. Igenewe kwibutsa `git`, ifise amategeko mato mato yo gukoresha amasezerano, kuyahamagara, gutanga itunga n'ibindi. Bitcoin Wallet ubu ntabwo iri muri iyo nkuru, ariko izoba iri mu nsiguro iri hafi (0.11). Iyi verisiyo ikurikira izotuma abakoresha bashobora gukora no gucunga amasakoshi yabo (biciye mu bisobanuro) kuva kuri `RGB`, harimwo n'ivya PSBT, guhuza n'ibikoresho vyo hanze (nk'akarorero Hardware Wallet) vyo gusinya, no gukorana na porogaramu nka Sparrow. Ivyo bizotuma igikorwa cose co gutanga no kwimurira umutungo coroha.


#### Gushiramwo biciye ku mizigo


Turashiramwo igikoresho muri Rust na:


```bash
cargo install rgb-contracts --all-features
```


(Iciyumviro: iyo sandugu yitwa `RGB-contracts`, kandi itegeko ryashizweho rizokwitwa `RGB`. Nimba iyo sandugu yitwa `RGB` iba yaramaze kubaho, hariho ugutombora, ni co gituma iryo zina)


Iryo shirwaho rikoranya umubare munini w'ibintu bishingiyeko (nk'ugusesangura amabwirizwa, gushiramwo Electrum, gucunga ibimenyamenya vy'ubumenyi zero, n'ibindi).


Igihe gushiramwo birangiye,:


```bash
rgb
```


Gukoresha `RGB` (ata mpamvu) yerekana urutonde rw'amabwirizwa mato ariho, nka `imirongo`, `Schema`, `kwinjiza`, `gusohora`, `ikibazo`, `Invoice`, `kwimurira ububiko`, n'ibindi. ibitabo, ibishushanyo n'ibishirwa mu ngiro), uhitemwo urubuga (Testnet, Mainnet) canke utunganye umukozi wawe wa Electrum.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/081.webp)


#### Incamake ya mbere y'ibigenzura


Iyo ukoresheje itegeko rikurikira, uzobona ko `RGB20` Interface isanzwe yinjijwe:


```bash
rgb interfaces
```


Niba iyi Interface idashizwemwo, kora clone ya:


```bash
git clone https://github.com/RGB-WG/rgb-interfaces
```


Bishire hamwe:


```bash
cargo run
```


Hanyuma ushiremwo Interface uhisemwo:


```bash
rgb import interfaces/RGB20.rgb
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/082.webp)


Ku rundi ruhande, tubwirwa ko ata Schema irashirwa muri iyo porogarama. Eka mbere nta Contract iri mu Stash. Kugira ngo uyibone, koresha itegeko:


```bash
rgb schemata
```


Ushobora rero gukora clone y'ububiko kugira ngo ubone ibishushanyo bimwe bimwe:


```bash
git clone https://github.com/RGB-WG/rgb-schemata
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/083.webp)


Ubu bubiko burimwo, mu bubiko bwayo bwa `src/`, amadosiye menshi ya Rust (nk'akarorero `nia.rs`) asobanura imirongo (NIA ku "*Itunga Ridashobora Gufutwa*", UDA ku "*Itunga ry'Igihugu*", n'ibindi). Kugira ngo ukoreshe, ushobora gukoresha:


```bash
cd rgb-schemata
cargo run
```


Ivyo bituma habaho amadosiye menshi `.RGB` na `.rgba` ahuye n'imirongo yashizwe hamwe. Nk'akarorero, uzosanga `Itunga ridashobora gutera.RGB`.


#### Kuzana ibicuruzwa vya Schema na Interface Implementation


Ubu ushobora kwinjiza igishushanyo muri `RGB`:


```bash
rgb import schemata/NonInflatableAssets.rgb
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/084.webp)


Ivyo bica biyongera kuri Stash yo mu karere. Nitwakoresha itegeko rikurikira, turabona ko Schema ubu ibonetse:


```bash
rgb schemata
```


### Contract irema (gusohora)


Hari uburyo bubiri bwo kurema umutungo mushasha:




- Canke dukoreshe inyandiko canke kode muri Rust yubaka Contract mu gushiramwo ivyicaro vya Schema (Global State, Ibihugu vy'Umutungo, n'ibindi) maze igatanga dosiye `.RGB` canke `.rgba`;
- Canke ukoreshe itegeko rito `issue` ataco rihinduye, n'idosiye ya YAML (canke TOML) idondora imiterere ya token.


Ushobora gusanga ingero muri Rust muri dosiye `ingero`, zigaragaza ingene wubaka `Uwukora Amasezerano`, wuzuze `Global State` (izina ry'umutungo, ikimenyetso, Supply, itariki, n'ibindi), usobanure Owned State (ivyo Owned State ari comp it muri vyose-1). *Contract Consignment* ushobora kwohereza hanze, kwemeza no kwinjiza mu Stash.


Ubundi buryo ni uguhindura n'amaboko dosiye ya YAML kugira ngo uhindure `ticker`, `izina`, `Supply`, n'ibindi. Twibaze ko dosiye yitwa `RGB20-demo.yaml`. Ushobora gusobanura:




- `spec`: ikimenyetso, izina, ukuri;
- `amajambo`: umwanya w'amatangazo y'amategeko;
- `Ivyasohowe`: umubare w'ama token yasohowe;
- `ibikorwa`: vyerekana Single-Use Seal (*Seal Definition*) n'ingero zifunguwe.


Aha ni akarorero ka dosiye ya YAML yo kurema:


```yaml
interface: RGB20Fixed

globals:
spec:
ticker: PBN
name: Plan B Network
details: "Pay attention: the asset has no value"
precision: 2
terms:
text: >
SUBJECT TO, AND WITHOUT IN ANY WAY LIMITING, THE REPRESENTATIONS AND WARRANTIES OF ANY SELLER. PROPERTY IS BEING SOLD “AS IS”...
media: ~
issuedSupply: 100000000

assignments:
assetOwner:
seal: tapret1st:b449f7eaa3f98c145b27ad0eeb7b5679ceb567faef7a52479bc995792b65f804:1
amount: 100000000 # this is 1 million (we have two digits for cents)
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/085.webp)


Hanyuma ukoreshe itegeko:


```bash
rgb issue '<SchemaID>' ssi:<Issuer> rgb20-demo.yaml
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/086.webp)


Ku bijanye nanje, ikimenyetso kidasanzwe ca Schema (kizoshirwa mu bimenyetso bimwe bimwe) ni `RDYhMTR! Rero itegeko ryanje ni:


```txt
rgb issue 'RDYhMTR!9gv8Y2GLv9UNBEK1hcrCmdLDFk9Qd5fnO8k' ssi:anonymous rgb20-demo.yaml
```


Niba utazi ID ya Schema, koresha itegeko:


```bash
rgb schemata
```


CLI yishura ko hariho Contract nshasha yasohowe kandi yongerwa ku Stash. Nitwandika iri tegeko rikurikira, turabona ko ubu hariho Contract y’inyongera, ihuye n’iyiherutse gusohoka:


```bash
rgb contracts
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/087.webp)


Hanyuma, itegeko rikurikira ryerekana ibihugu vyo kw’isi yose (izina, ikimenyetso, Supply...) n’urutonde rw’ibihugu vy’ubutunzi, ni ukuvuga ivy’ugutanga (nk’akarorero, ibimenyetso vy’imiliyoni 1 `PBN` vyasobanuwe muri UTXO `b449f7eaa3f98c145b27ad0eeb7b5679ceb567faef7a52479bc995792b65f804:1`).


```bash
rgb state '<ContractId>'
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/088.webp)


### Gusohora hanze, kwinjiza mu gihugu no kwemeza


Kugira ngo usangire iyi Contract n'abandi bakoresha, ushobora kuyirungika hanze kuva kuri Stash ikaja kuri:


```bash
rgb export '<ContractId>' myContractPBN.rgb
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/089.webp)


Dosiye `myContractPBN.RGB` ishobora gushikirizwa uwundi mukozi, ashobora kuyishira kuri Stash yiwe n'itegeko:


```bash
rgb import myContractPBN.rgb
```


Ku bijanye no kwinjiza, nimba ari *Contract Consignment* yoroshe, tuzoronka ubutumwa "`Kuzana Consignment RGB`". Niba ari *State Transition Consignment* nini, itegeko rizoba ritandukanye (`RGB yemera`).


Kugira ngo umenye neza ko ari ukuri, ushobora kandi gukoresha igikorwa co kwemeza co mu karere. Nk'akarorero, woshobora kwiruka:


```bash
rgb validate myContract.rgb
```


#### Stash ikoreshwa, kugenzura no kugaragaza


Nk’ukwibutsa, Stash ni urutonde rw’ibintu vyo mu karere vy’imirongo, imirongo, ishyirwa mu ngiro n’amasezerano (Genesis + imihindukire). Igihe cose ukoresheje "import", wongerako ikintu kuri Stash. Iyi Stash ishobora kurabwa mu buryo burambuye n’itegeko:


```bash
rgb dump
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/090.webp)


Ivyo bizotuma generate igira dosiye irimwo amakuru yose ya Stash.


### Kwimurira na PSBT


Kugira ngo ukore ukwimurira, uzokenera gukoresha Bitcoin Wallet yo mu karere kugira ngo ucungere amasezerano ya `Tapret` canke `Opret`.


#### 2013 na 2014


Akenshi, ugukorana hagati y’abaje mu nama y’ubuhinga bwa none (nk’akarorero, Alice na Bob) bibera biciye mu guhingura Invoice. Iyo Alice ashaka ko Bob akora ikintu (kwimurira token, gusubira gusohora, igikorwa muri DAO, n'ibindi), Alice irema Invoice idondora amabwirizwa yiwe kuri Bob. Rero dufise:




- **Igitabu-2021** (uwatanze igitabu-2020);
- **Bob** (ni we yakira kandi agashitsa Invoice).


Mu buryo butandukanye n’ibindi bidukikije, RGB Invoice ntigarukira ku ciyumviro co kwishura gusa. Ishobora gushiramwo igisabwa cose gifitaniye isano na Contract: gukuraho urufunguzo, gutora, gukora igicapo (*igicapo*) kuri NFT, n'ibindi. Ivyo bishobora gusobanurwa muri Contract Interface.


Itegeko rikurikira ritanga RGB Invoice:


```bash
$ rgb invoice $CONTRACT -i $INTERFACE $ACTION $STATE $SEAL
```


Hamwe:




- `$Contract`: Ikimenyetso ca Contract (*Id y'Isezerano*);
- `$Interface`: Interface izokoreshwa (nk'akarorero `RGB20`);
- `$ACTION`: izina ry'igikorwa kigaragazwa muri Interface (ku bijanye n'uguhindura token, ivyo bishobora kuba "Ukwimurira"). Niba Interface isanzwe itanga igikorwa c'imbere, ntukeneye kugisubiramwo hano;
- `$STATE`: amakuru y'imimerere azokwimurirwa (nk'akarorero, umubare w'ibimenyetso iyo token ishobora guhinduka irungitswe);
- `$Seal`: Single-Use Seal y'uwuronka inyungu (Alice), ni ukuvuga ivyerekeye UTXO. Bob izokoresha aya makuru kugira ngo yubake Witness Transaction, kandi igisubizo gihuye kizoba ica Alice (mu *blinded UTXO* canke mu buryo butagiramwo amakuru).


Nk’akarorero, n’amabwirizwa akurikira .


```bash
alice$ CONTRACT='iZgIN9EL-2H21UgQ-x!A3uJc-WwXhCSm-$9Lwcc1-v!mUkKY'
alice$ MY_UTXO=4960acc21c175c551af84114541eace09c14d3a1bb184809f7b80916f57f9ef8:1
alice$ rgb invoice $CONTRACT -i RGB20 --amount 100 $MY_UTXO
```


Igikoresho ca CLI kizoba igikoresho ca generate na Invoice nk'iki:


```bash
rgb:iZgIN9EL-2H21UgQ-x!A3uJc-WwXhCSm-$9Lwcc1-v!mUkKY/RGB20/100+utxob:zlVS28Rb-...
```


Ishobora gushikirizwa Bob biciye ku nzira iyo ari yo yose (inyandiko, kode ya QR, n’ibindi).


#### Kwimurira


Kugira ngo ushiremwo iyi Invoice:




- Bob (uwufise ibimenyetso muri Stash yiwe) afise Bitcoin Wallet. Arakeneye gutegura igikorwa co gucuruza Bitcoin (mu buryo bwa PSBT, nk’akarorero `tx.PSBT`) gikoresha ama UTXO aho ibimenyetso vya RGB bisabwa biri, yongerako UTXO imwe y’amahera (PSBT);
- Bob ikora itegeko rikurikira:


```bash
bob$ rgb transfer tx.psbt $INVOICE consignment.rgb
```




- Ibi bitanga dosiye `Consignment.RGB` irimwo:
 - Amateka y’ihinduka yerekana Alice ko ivyo bimenyetso ari ivy’ukuri;
 - Ihinduka rishasha ryimurira ibimenyetso kuri Single-Use Seal ya Alice;
 - Igitabo ca Witness Transaction (kitashizweko umukono).
- Bob yohereza iyi dosiye `Consignment.RGB` kuri Alice (biciye kuri e-mail, kuri server yo gusangira canke kuri porotokole ya RGB-RPC, Igihuhusi, n'ibindi);
- Alice yakira `Consignment.RGB` kandi ikayemera muri Stash yayo bwite:


```bash
alice$ rgb accept consignment.rgb
```




- CLI isuzuma ukuri kw'ihinduka maze ikayongera kuri Stash ya Alice. Iyo ataco bimaze, itegeko rirananirwa n'ubutumwa bw'ikosa burambuye. Ahandi ho, biraroranirwa, kandi bikavuga ko iyo nzira y’ugucuruza y’akarorero itaratangazwa ku rubuga rwa Bitcoin (Bob irindiriye umuco wa Green wa Alice);
- Mu buryo bwo kwemeza, itegeko `kwemera` rigarura umukono (*payslip*) Alice ashobora kohereza Bob kugira ngo amwereke ko yemeje *Consignment*;
- Bob ashobora rero gusinya no gutangaza (`--tangaza`) ibikorwa vyiwe vya Bitcoin:


```bash
bob$ rgb check <sig> && wallet sign --publish tx.psbt
```




- Igihe iyo nzira yemejwe On-Chain, Ownership y'umutungo ifatwa nk'iyimuriwe kuri Alice. Alice ya Wallet, igenzura Mining y'isoko, ibona Owned State nshasha iboneka muri Stash yayo.


Mu gice gikurikira, tuzokwihweza neza ingene RGB yoshirwa muri Lightning Network.


## RGB kuri Lightning Network


<chapterId>0962980a-8f94-5d0f-9cd0-43d7f884a01d</chapterId>


:::id ya videwo=be25a165-6e23-488c-91d8-3dcfccc6eca1:::


Muri iki gice, ndasaba gusuzuma ingene RGB ishobora gukoreshwa muri Lightning Network, mu gushiramwo no kwimurira ivy’ubutunzi bwa RGB (ibimenyetso, NFT, n’ibindi) biciye mu nzira zo kwishura za off-chain.


Iciyumviro nyamukuru ni uko RGB State Transition (*State Transition*) ishobora kwiyemeza gukora igikorwa ca Bitcoin, na co nyene, gishobora kuguma ari off-chain gushika umurongo w’umuravyo ufunze. Rero, igihe cose umurongo uvuguruwe, RGB State Transition nshasha irashobora kwinjizwa mu gikorwa gishasha co gukora, ivyo bikaba bica bihindura ubusa iyo mpinduka ya kera. Muri ubwo buryo, imirongo ya Lightning irashobora gukoreshwa mu gutanga itunga rya RGB, kandi ishobora gukoreshwa mu buryo bumwe n’ubw’amahera asanzwe ya Lightning.


### Guhingura umurongo no gutanga amafaranga


Kugira ngo dukore umurongo w’umuravyo utwara ivy’ubutunzi vya RGB, turakeneye Elements zibiri:




- Bitcoin infashanyo yo kurema 2/2 Multisig y’umurongo (UTXO y’ishimikiro y’umurongo);
- RGB infashanyo, yohereza itunga kuri Multisig nyene.


Mu majambo ya Bitcoin, igikorwa co gutanga amahera kigomba kubaho kugira ngo gisobanure igipimo ca UTXO, naho coba kirimwo gusa umubare mutoyi wa Sats (ni ikibazo gusa c’umusaruro wose mu bikorwa vya Commitment vyo muri kazoza bisigaye hejuru y’umupaka wa Dust wose same). Nk’akarorero, Alice ishobora gufata ingingo yo gutanga 10k Sats na 500 USDT (itangazwa nk’umutungo wa RGB). Ku bijanye n'ugutanga amahera, twongerako Commitment (`Opret` canke `Tapret`) ishingira intahe RGB State Transition.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/091.webp)


Igihe igikorwa co gutanga amahera kimaze gutegurwa (ariko kitaratangazwa), igikorwa ca Commitment kiraremwa kugira ngo umwe wese mu bagize uruhande ashobore gufunga umuhora ku ruhande rumwe igihe cose. Ivyo bikorwa bisa n'ivyo Commitment vya kera vya Lightning, kiretse ko twongerako ikindi gisohoka kirimwo RGB Anchor (OP_RETURN canke Taproot) gihuye n'iyi State Transition nshasha.


RGB State Transition rero ijana umutungo kuva kuri 2/2 Multisig y'infashanyo ikaja ku biva muri Commitment Transaction. Ivyiza vy’iyi nzira ni uko umutekano w’igihugu ca RGB uhuye neza n’ubuhinga bwo guhana bwa Lightning: iyo Bob itangaje igihugu c’umurongo wa kera, Alice irashobora kumuhana no gukoresha igisohoka, kugira ngo isubire ku Sats n’ivyo vyose. Ico kintu gitera intege rero kirakomeye kuruta mbere n’ico mu muhora wa Lightning udafise itunga rya RGB, kuko uwutera ashobora gutakaza atari Sats gusa, ariko kandi n’itunga rya RGB ry’uwo muhora.


Commitment Transaction yashizweko umukono na Alice ikarungikwa kuri Bob rero yoba imeze gutya:


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/092.webp)


Kandi Commitment Transaction iherekejwe, yashizweko umukono na Bob ikarungikwa kuri Alice, izomera gutya:


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/093.webp)


### Ivugurura ry'umurongo


Iyo habayeho ukwishyura hagati y’abafatanyabikorwa babiri (canke bipfuza guhindura ugutanga umutungo), barema umugwi mushasha w’ibikorwa vya Commitment. Amafaranga ari muri Sats ku giciro cose ashobora canke ntahinduke, bivanye n’ugushirwa mu ngiro, kuko uruhara rwayo nyamukuru ari ugutuma habaho kwubaka UTXO zifise akamaro. Ku rundi ruhande, igisohoka ca OP_RETURN (canke Taproot) kigomba guhindurwa kugira ngo kibemwo RGB Anchor nshasha, igereranya ugusangira gushasha kw’itunga mu muyoboro.


Nk’akarorero, iyo Alice yohereje amadolari 30 kuri Bob mu muyoboro, State Transition nshasha izokwerekana amadolari 400 ku Alice n’amadolari 100 ku Bob. Igikorwa kijanye n'ugusezerana congerwa kuri (canke gihindurwa na) OP_RETURN/Taproot Anchor kugira ngo kigiremwo iyo mpinduka. Zirikana ko, uhereye ku mbonerahamwe ya RGB, ivyo winjiza mu guhindura biguma ari Multisig ya mbere (aho itunga rya On-Chain rihabwa mu vy’ukuri gushika umuyoboro ufunze). Ivyo RGB isohora (ivy’ugutanga) vyonyene ni vyo bihinduka, bivanye n’ugusubira gusangira vyafashwe ingingo.


Igitabo ca Commitment Transaction cashizweko umukono na Alice, giteguwe gukwiragizwa na Bob:


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/094.webp)


Igitabo ca Commitment Transaction cashizweko umukono na Bob, giteguwe gukwiragizwa na Alice:


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/095.webp)


### Ubuyobozi bwa HTLC


Mu vy’ukuri, Lightning Network iratuma amahera yishurwa ashobora guca mu nzira nyinshi, hakoreshejwe HTLCs (*Amasezerano Apfungiwe n’Igihe*). Ni ko biri no kuri RGB: ku kwishura kwose guca mu muhora, umusaruro wa HTLC wongerwa ku gucuruza, n'ugutanga RGB guhuye n'iyi HTLC. Gutyo, uwuzokoresha umusaruro wa HTLC (bivuye ku banga canke inyuma y’aho igihe co gufunga kirangiriye) arasubirana Sats n’itunga ry’i RGB rijana na ryo. Ku rundi ruhande, biragaragara ko ukeneye kugira amahera ahagije ku nzira mu bijanye n’itunga ryompi Sats na RGB.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/096.webp)


Ivyo RGB ikora kuri Lightning rero bitegerezwa gufatwa nk’uko bihuye n’ivyo Lightning Network ubwayo ikora. Niba wifuza kwihweza cane muri iki cigwa, ndagusavye cane ko uraba iyindi nyigisho yuzuye:


https://planb.network/courses/34bd43ef-6683-4a5c-b239-7cb1e40a4aeb

### Ikarata ya kode ya RGB


Ubwa nyuma, imbere yo kuja mu gice gikurikira, ndashaka kubaha icegeranyo c'itegeko rikoreshwa muri RGB. Iryo tegeko rishingiye ku masomero ya Rust n’ibisobanuro vy’inkomoko yuguruye. Aha niho hari insiguro y'ububiko nyamukuru n'amasandugu:


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/097.webp)


#### Client-side Validation




- **Ububiko**: [kwemeza_uruhande rw'umukiriya](https://github.com/LNP-BP/kwemeza_uruhande_rw'umukiriya)
- **Amasandugu**: [kwemeza_uruhande_rw'umukiriya](https://amasandugu.io/amasandugu/kwemeza_uruhande rw'umukiriya), [ibimenyetso_bikoreshwa_rimwe](https://amasandugu.io/amasandugu/ibimenyetso_bikoreshwa_rimwe)


Uburongozi bw’ukwemeza off-chain n’ubuhinga bwo gukoresha rimwe Seals.


#### Ivyemezo vy'Itegeko Bitcoin (DBC)




- **Ububiko**: [Ishingiro rya bp] (Ishingiro ry'Igihugu)
- **Isandugu**: [bp-dbc](https://isanduku.io/isanduku/bp-dbc)


Uburongozi bw’ugushinga intahe mu bikorwa vya Bitcoin (Tapret, OP_RETURN, n’ibindi).


#### Multi Protocol Commitment (MPC)




- **Ububiko**: [kwemeza_uruhande rw'umukiriya](https://github.com/LNP-BP/kwemeza_uruhande_rw'umukiriya)
- **Isandugu**: [gusuzuma_gukora](https://ibisandugu.io/ibisanduka/ugusuzuma_gukora)


Ivyiyumviro vyinshi vy’ugukorana n’ugushiramwo n’amategeko atandukanye.


#### Ubwoko bukomeye n'ugushiramwo amakuru




- **Ibisobanuro**: [urubuga ubwoko-bukomeye.org](https://www.ubwoko-bukomeye.org/)
- **Ububiko**: [ubwoko-bukomeye](https://github.com/ubwoko-bukomeye/ubwoko-bukomeye), [gushiramwo-bukomeye](https://github.com/ubwoko-bukomeye/gushiramwo-bukomeye)
- **Amasandugu**: [ubwoko_bukomeye](https://amasandugu.io/amasandugu/ubwoko_bukomeye), [gushiramwo_amakode](https://amasandugu.io/amasandugu/gushiramwo_amakode)


Uburyo bwo kwandika bukomeye n'urutonde rw'ibintu bikoreshwa kuri Client-side Validation.


#### RGB Ishingiro




- **Ububiko**: [RGB-ishingiro](RGB-Ishingiro)
- **Isanduku**: [RGB-umutima](https://isanduku.io/isanduku/RGB-umutima)


Ishingiro ry’iyo porotokole, rigizwe n’intumbero nyamukuru y’ukwemeza RGB.


#### RGB Ububiko bw'ibitabu busanzwe & Wallet




- **Ububiko**: [Ububiko-2178-ububiko](Ububiko).
- **Isandugu**: [RGB-std](igisandugu.io/isanduku/RGB-igisandugu)


Ivyiyumviro vy’ugushirwa mu ngiro, uburongozi bwa Stash na Wallet.


#### RGB CLI




- **Ububiko**: [Ububiko-2184](Ububiko).
- **Amasandugu**: [RGB-CLI] (Isanduku.io/Isandugu/RGB-CLI), [Isandugu-2187-2185]


Ivyo bikoresho bikoreshwa mu gukoresha amasezerano.


#### RGB Schema




- **Ububiko**: [Imirongo ya RGB] (Imirongo ya RGB/Imirongo ya RGB/)


Irimwo ingero z’imirongo (NIA, UDA, n’ibindi) n’ingene zishirwa mu ngiro.


#### AluVM




- **Amakuru**: [AluVM.org](urubuga rwacu-2195.org/)
- **Ububiko**: [Ibisobanuro vya AluVM](Ibisobanuro vya AluVM), [Ivyiyumviro](Ivyiyumviro)
- **Amasandugu**: [AluVM](amasandugu.io/amasandugu/AluVM), [amasandugu](amasandugu.io/amasandugu/amasandugu)


Igikoresho gishingiye ku kwandika gikoreshwa mu gukoresha inyandiko zo kwemeza.


#### Amasezerano ya Bitcoin - BP




- **Ububiko**: [bp-core] (bp-core), [bp-std] (bp-std), [bp-gW-2199](bp-gw-2199)


Ivyongeyeko vyo gushigikira umurongo wa Bitcoin (ibikorwa, ivy’uguca mu nzira, n’ibindi).


#### Ivy'Ibarabara ry'Ivy'Ibarabara - UBIDECO




- **Ububiko**: [UBIDECO](UBIDECO)


Ibidukikije bifitaniye isano n’iterambere ry’ivy’ubuhinga ry’inkomoko yuguruye.


# Inyubakwa kuri RGB


<partId>3b4b0d66-0c1b-505a-b5ca-4b2e57dd73c2</partId>


## DIBA n'umugambi wa Bitmask


<chapterId>dc92a5e8-ed93-5a3f-bcd0-d433932842f4</chapterId>


:::id ya videwo=2ec9a181-a8b0-4da2-b7b5-9dfaaeb10ba:::


Iki gice ca nyuma c’amashure gishingiye ku nsiguro zashikirijwe n’abatanga insiguro batandukanye mu nama y’ivyigwa ya RGB. Harimwo intahe n’ivyiyumviro ku RGB n’ibidukikije vyayo, hamwe n’ugushikiriza ibikoresho n’imigambi ishingiye kuri iyo porotokole. Iki gice ca mbere kirongowe na Hunter Beast, ibindi bibiri bikurikira na Frederico Tenga.


### Kuva ku nyandiko ya Java gushika kuri Rust, no mu bidukikije vya Bitcoin


Mu ntango, Hunter Beast yakora cane cane mu rurimi rw’igifaransa. Hanyuma abona **Rust**, insiguro y’amajambo yayo yasa n’iyidashimishije kandi ibabaza mu ntango. Ariko rero, yaraje gutahura ububasha bw’ururimi, ukugenzura ubwonko (*heap* na *stack*), n’umutekano n’ubushobozi bijana na vyo. Ashimika ku vy’uko Rust ari ikibanza ciza cane co kwimenyerezamwo kugira ngo umuntu atahure bimwe bigera kure ingene orodinateri ikora.


Hunter Beast avuga ivy’amateka yiwe mu migambi itandukanye mu bidukikije *Altcoin*, nka Ethereum (ifise ubukomezi, TypeScript, n’ibindi), hanyuma Filecoin. Asigura ko mu ntango yatangajwe n’amasezerano amwe amwe, ariko amaherezo yumva ko menshi muri yo yamuhemukiye, atari kubera ubuhinga bwayo bwo gukoresha ibimenyetso. Aragaya inkurikizi z’amahera ziteye amakenga, uguhingura ibimenyetso vy’ugutera imbere bitera ubwoba abashoramari, n’umuce ushobora gutuma iyo migambi ikoreshwa nabi. Yaciye rero aheza afata ingingo ya **Bitcoin Maximalist**, atari ukubera ko hari abantu bamwebamwe bamufunguriye amaso ku buryo bwiza bw’ubutunzi bwa Bitcoin, no ku gukomera kw’iyi nzira.


### Ugusaba kwa RGB no kwubaka ku bipande


Ico camujijuye ata gukeka ko Bitcoin ifise akamaro, mu majambo yiwe, ni ukuvumbura RGB be n’iciyumviro c’ibice. Yemera ko ibikorwa biriho ku bindi bice vy’umubiri bishobora gusubirwamwo ku bice vy’imbere, hejuru ya Bitcoin, ata guhindura umurongo w’ishimikiro.


Muri Ruhuhuma 2022, yinjiye muri **DIBA** kugira ngo akore cane cane kuri RGB, na cane cane kuri **Bitmask** Wallet. Iciyo gihe, Bitmask yari ikiri kuri verisiyo 0.01 kandi yariko ikoresha RGB kuri verisiyo 0.4, gusa ku bijanye no gucunga ibimenyetso bimwe bimwe. Avuga ko ivyo vyari bishingiye cane ku kwizigama nk’uko biri muri iki gihe, kuko ivyiyumviro vyari bishingiye ku serveri. Kuva ico gihe, ubwubatsi bwarateye imbere buja kuri iyo nzira, ishimwa cane n’aba bitcoiners.


### Ishingiro ry'amasezerano ya RGB


Itegeko rya **RGB** ni ryo rishasha kandi riteye imbere cane ry'iciyumviro c'ibiceri vy'amabara, ryaramaze gusuzumwa nko mu 2012-2013. Iciyo gihe, amashirahamwe menshi yariko ararondera gufatanya agaciro gatandukanye ka Bitcoin ku UTXO, ivyo vyatumye habaho ugushirwa mu ngiro kwinshi gutatanijwe. Ukwo kutagira urugero n’ugusaba guke ico gihe vyatumye ivyo bisubizo bitaronka ikibanza kiramvye.


Ubu, RGB irahagaze kubera ubukomezi bwayo bw’ivyiyumviro n’ibisobanuro vy’ubumwe biciye ku shirahamwe rya LNP/BP. Iryo hame rishingiye kuri Client-side Validation. Bitcoin Blockchain ibika gusa amasezerano y’ubuhinga bwa none (_amasezerano_, biciye kuri Taproot canke OP_RETURN), mu gihe amakuru menshi (insobanuro za Contract, amateka yo kwimurira, n’ibindi) abikwa n’abakoresha bireba. Muri ubwo buryo, umuzigo wo kubika uragabanywa kandi ibanga ry’uguhanahana rirakomezwa, ata kuremerera Blockchain. Ubu buryo burashoboza kurema ibintu bishobora guhinduka (**RGB20** standard) canke ibintu bidasanzwe (**RGB21**), mu rwego rw’ibice kandi bishobora guhindurwa.


### Ibikorwa vya token (RGB20) n'ibintu bidasanzwe (RGB21)


Na **RGB20**, dusobanura token ishobora guhinduka kuri Bitcoin. Uwutanga amafaranga ahitamwo _ugutanga_, _ugutanga_, agaca akora _amasezerano_ ashobora guca akoramwo amafaranga. Igihe cose umuntu yimuriwe, akoresheje Bitcoin UTXO, ikora nk’igitabu *Single-Use Seal*. Ivyo bituma uwukoresha atazoshobora gukoresha umutungo umwe incuro zibiri, kuko umuntu wenyene ashobora gukoresha UTXO ari we afise urufunguzo rwo guhindura uko Contract iri ku ruhande rw'umukiriya.


**RGB21** igamije ivy'ubutunzi bidasanzwe (canke "NFT"). Ico kintu gifise Supply ya 1, kandi gishobora gufatanywa n’amakuru (dosiye y’amashusho, amajwi, n’ibindi) adondora biciye mu kibanza kinaka. Udakunze NFTs ku blockchains za bose, amakuru n’ibimenyetso vyayo vya MIME birashobora kuguma ari ivy’ibanga, bigakwiragizwa n’abandi ku bushake bwa nyen’ivyo bikoresho.


### Umuti w'ibipfukisho: Wallet ku RGB


Kugira ngo ubushobozi bwa RGB bukoreshwe mu bikorwa, umugambi wa **DIBA** warateguye Wallet yitwa [Bitmask](https://bitmask.app/). Iciyumviro ni ugutanga igikoresho kitagira ububiko, gishingiye kuri Taproot, gishobora gushikwako nk’urubuga canke nk’igikoresho co kwagura umucukumbuzi. Bitmask icungera ivy'ubutunzi vya RGB20 na RGB21, kandi igashiramwo uburyo butandukanye bwo gucungera umutekano:




- Itegeko ry’ishimikiro ryanditswe muri Rust, hanyuma rikakoranywa muri WebAssembly kugira ngo rikore mu bidukikije vya JavaScript (React);
- Imfunguruzo ziterwa mu karere, hanyuma zigabikwa zipfutse mu karere;
- Amakuru ya Leta (Stash) abikwa mu mutwe, akurikiranwa kandi ashirwa mu mfuruka biciye mu bubiko bw'ibitabu bwa **Carbonado**, bukora igikorwa co gufatanya, gukosora amakosa, gupfuka no kugenzura uruzi hakoreshejwe Blake3.


Kubera iyo nyubakwa, ibikorwa vyose vy’ubutunzi bibera ku ruhande rw’umukiriya. Uvuye hanze, igikorwa ca Bitcoin nta kindi ariko ni igikorwa ca kera co gukoresha amahera ca Taproot, ata n’umwe yokwikeka ko na co nyene gifise uguhindura ibimenyetso canke NFTs. Kuba ata On-Chain irengeje urugero (nta metadata ibitswe ku mugaragaro) biremeza urugero runaka rw’ubukerebutsi kandi bituma vyoroha kunanira ukugerageza gucengera gushoboka.


### Umutekano n'ubwubatsi busanzwe


Kubera ko umurongo wa RGB usaba ko uwuriko arakora wese aguma afise amateka y’ibikorwa vyiwe (kugira ngo yerekane ko amafaranga yimuriwe ari ay’ukuri), ikibazo co kubika kiravyuka. Bitmask isaba gushiramwo iyi Stash mu karere, hanyuma ikayirungika ku ma server menshi canke ku bicu (ntibikenewe). Amakuru aguma apfutse n'uwukoresha biciye kuri **Carbonado**, rero umukozi ntashobora kuyasoma. Iyo habayeho ugusenyuka kw’igice, ugukosora amakosa Layer kurashobora gusubiramwo ibirimwo.


Ikoreshwa rya CRDT (_Ubwoko bw'amakuru asubiyemwo ata ntambara_) rituma verisiyo zitandukanye za Stash zishobora guhurizwa hamwe, iyo zishobora gutandukana. Umuntu wese arafise umwidegemvyo wo kwakira ayo makuru aho yipfuza hose, kuko ata Full node n’imwe itwara amakuru yose afitaniye isano n’ico kintu. Ivyo vyerekana neza na neza filozofiya ya *Client-side Validation*, aho nyen’umutungo wese afise inshingano yo kubika ibimenyamenya vy’ukuri kw’umutungo wiwe wa RGB.


### Ku bijanye n'ibidukikije vyagutse: isoko, ugukorana n'abandi n'ibikorwa bishasha


Ishirahamwe riri inyuma ya Bitmask ntirigarukira ku gutegura Wallet. DIBA ifise umugambi wo gutegura:




- **Isoko** ryo guhanahana ibimenyetso, cane cane mu buryo bwa **RGB21**;
- Guhuza n’ibindi bikoresho (nk’ivyo *Iris Wallet*);
- Ubuhinga bwo kwimurira amafaranga, ni ukuvuga ubushobozi bwo gushiramwo amafaranga menshi akurikirana ya RGB mu gucuruza kumwe.


Muri ico gihe nyene, turiko turakora ku **WebBTC** canke **WebLN** (ingingo ngenderwako zishoboza imbuga gusaba Wallet gusinya amasezerano ya Bitcoin canke Lightning), hamwe n'ubushobozi bwo "gukoresha televiziyo" ivyinjijwe vya Bitcoin (niba dushaka gusubiza mu gihugu ca Wallet).


### Iciyumviro


Ivyo vyose vyerekana ingene ubuhinga bwa RGB bushobora gukoreshwa no gushikira abakoresha biciye mu gutorera umuti ibibazo bikomeye. Ihinduka kuva ku mbonerahamwe ya Altcoin gushika ku mbonerahamwe ishingiye kuri Bitcoin, hamwe n’ukuvumbura *Client-side Validation*, vyerekana inzira yumvikana neza: turatahura ko bishoboka gushirwa mu ngiro ibikorwa bitandukanye (ibimenyetso bishobora guhinduka, NFT, amasezerano y’ubwenge ya GW by-5...) ata2. y'imihigo y'ibanga ku bikorwa vya Taproot canke OP_RETURNs.


**Bitmask** Wallet ni kimwe muri iyo nzira: ku ruhande rwa Blockchain, ivyo ubona vyose ni ugucuruza kwa Bitcoin gusanzwe; ku ruhande rw'ukoresha, ukoresha urubuga Interface aho urema, Exchange kandi ukabika ubwoko bwose bw'itunga rya off-chain. Ico kigereranyo gitandukanya neza ibikorwa remezo vy’amahera (Bitcoin) n’ubuhinga bwo gutanga no gutanga (RGB), mu gihe kigaragaza urugero rwo hejuru rw’ibanga n’ugushobora gutera imbere neza.


## Ibikorwa vya Bitfinex kuri RGB


<chapterId>d4d80e07-5eac-5b29-a93a-123180e97047</chapterId>


:::id ya videwo=04555813-516f-4eea-9767-7082c2ea6f01:::


Muri iki gice, twisunze ikiganiro ca Frederico Tenga, turaba urutonde rw’ibikoresho n’imigambi yashizweho n’umugwi wa Bitfinex wiyeguriye RGB, n’intumbero yo guteza imbere uguseruka kw’ibidukikije vy’ubutunzi kandi bitandukanye bikikuje iyo porotokole. Intumbero y’intango y’iryo tsinda si ugusohora igicuruzwa c’ubudandaji kinaka, ahubwo ni ugutanga ibice vy’inyubako vya porogarama, gutanga umusanzu ku masezerano ya RGB ubwayo, no gutanga ibimenyetso vy’ukuri vyo gushirwa mu ngiro nk’igikoresho gigendagenda (*Iris Wallet*) canke igikoresho gishobora gukoreshwa na RGB-com.


### Inyuma n'intumbero


Kuva nko mu mwaka w’2022, ikigo ca Bitfinex RGB caramaze kwibanda ku gutegura urutonde rw’ubuhinga bufasha RGB gukoreshwa no kugeragezwa neza. Hariho intererano nyinshi zatanzwe:
